During the Xi'an Incident, the Traitorous Bandits in Chahar Province Eagerly Sought to Stir Up Trouble: A Certain Chief of a Special Service Organ Convened a Meeting of Puppet Leaders, Deciding to Seize the Opportunity to Counterattack Liangmiao and Re-Offend Wuchuan and Guyang 76

Zhangbei correspondence: Since the outbreak of the border defense war in Suiyuan on November 12 of this year, the National Army has achieved successive victories. In less than a month, it was able to recover Liangmiao (Bailingmiao and D庙). As soon as the fighting began, it terrified the traitorous bandits. Some were temporarily forced to agree, and many defected to our side. Under the leadership of the leader of the unified national country, the people of the whole country hoped that the National Army would launch a large-scale campaign to eliminate the bandits' lair and recover the lost territories. Unexpectedly, the Xi'an Incident occurred, which was not only a major blow to the country's progress, but also an excellent opportunity for the traitorous bandits to harm the country. This shocking news, upon reaching northern Chahar on the 12th, caused millions of people awaiting rescue to be filled with dismay and anxiety. During this serious period of the incident, there was indeed news that the traitorous bandits were taking the opportunity to stir up trouble. According to a certain gentleman who came to Zhangbei from Jiabusi Temple on the 15th, Prince De had left Bailingmiao for Xisunit Banner on November 22nd, and was recuperating at the palace. The news of the Xi'an rebellion was learned by a certain chief of a special service organ stationed in Jiabusi Temple on the 12th. He immediately telegraphed Prince De and the Mongol puppet military leaders Bao Yueqing, Zhuo Shihai, Li Shouxin, etc., ordering them to depart immediately and gather at Jiabusi Temple on the 13th for an important consultation. Prince De had originally planned to return to Jiabusi Temple on the 14th, but after receiving the telegram from the chief of the special service organ, he advanced his departure from the Xisunit Banner Palace to the 13th and rushed to Jiabusi Temple. Li Shouxin, Bao Yueqing, Zhuo Shihai, and others also rushed from their respective defense areas at the same time. That evening, a meeting was held under the chairmanship of the chief of the special service organ, and it did not end until late at night. The personnel participating in this important meeting on the evening of the 13th included, in addition to the chief of the special service organ, a certain councilor of the puppet Mongolian government and various commanders on the one hand. On the other hand, the traitorous bandits included Prince De, Zhuo Shihai, Bao Yueqing, Li Shouxin, and other puppets. The results of the meeting generally decided to take advantage of the unresolved Xi'an Incident to actively reorganize the military and attack westward: (1) Still using Prince De's Mongolian army, Bao Yueqing, Zhuo Shihai, etc., as the main force, supplemented by a small number of troops from the Rehe puppet army, to counterattack D庙 and Bailingmiao, and to peep westward at Guyang and Wuchuan in northern Suiyuan. (2) Li Shouxin's puppet army and Zhang Haipeng's troops from Rehe to capture Taolin in eastern Suiyuan. (3) Zhang Wanqing's bandit army and Gan Jingxiu's troops from Rehe to attack Xinghe, using their regular army as support for all routes, and commanding everything. At the same time, it was also agreed that Prince De and the puppet Mongolian military generals, such as Li and Bao, would jointly request the ×× army to allocate aircraft, tanks, and other weapons. The reason is that when the ×× side saw the bandits and puppets constantly defecting, it transferred all the tanks and aircraft that had been allocated to the bandits and puppets back to Duolun, so they requested that they be returned to increase their strength. The date of the general attack has not yet been decided, but all units are being urged to quickly reorganize their troops and prepare food. Li Shouxin, Bao Yueqing, Zhuo Shihai, and other officers who went to the temple for the meeting are required to leave the temple on the 16th and 17th and return to their original defenses to prepare everything.

Rice Prices in Guangdong Province Rising Daily: Authorities Telegraph Guangxi Province to Lift Rice Ban for Relief; Banking Sector Sends Personnel to Investigate Hunan Rice Production and Sales 77

Guangzhou correspondence: Rice prices in Guangdong Province have been soaring recently, and have not shown any signs of declining. Those concerned about the current situation believe this is a serious social problem. The authorities previously telegraphed the central government to temporarily abolish the foreign rice tax in order to stabilize market prices. Later, the Finance Department also gathered five million yuan from the banking sector to organize a civil food agency to purchase rice from Jiangxi and Hunan Provinces for sale in Guangdong Province, so as to prevent the outflow of interests. Although the above two methods differ in approach, their purpose is the same: to relieve the people's food supply. According to people in the rice industry, the fundamental reason for the recent high rice prices in Guangdong Province is the poor harvest of late rice. At the same time, the governments of various counties are strictly implementing grain storage for famine preparedness, so that local grain is barely enough for self-sufficiency in each county. Areas that used to have surplus rice and rice flowing to the cities are now in a state of restricted sales. Therefore, the current situation, whether in rural areas or cities, is that the demand for grain exceeds the supply. Moreover, the imported rice from neighboring provinces is not as sufficient as before. The Anhui Province Yanhuzhen Jiangmi rice, due to the province's ban on rice exports, has almost completely cut off the route to Guangdong. Although Guangdong merchants have recently purchased Hunan rice in Changsha, transportation is difficult. The direct train on the Guangdong-Hankou Railway from Guangzhou to Wuhan cannot transport Hunan rice southward in large quantities due to a shortage of vehicles. Although Guangdong rice merchants stationed in Changsha have purchased and stored more than 100,000 bags of grain, the Guangdong-Hankou Railway cannot transport them all at once. If they want to change to waterway transportation to Guangdong, the freight is too high, making it uneconomical for trade. Therefore, a large batch of Hunan rice has still not been able to relieve the current market's thirst. As for Guangxi Province, it has always been a rice-rich area. In the past, Wuzhou rice transportation to Guangdong was one of the largest export commodities. In recent years, due to the turbulence in Guangxi Province, food control has been implemented, and grain is still being actively stored, and the rice ban has not been lifted. Therefore, Guangdong Province, which usually relies on Guangxi rice for supply, has been cut off again since autumn and winter. This is another reason for the shortage of grain in Guangdong. Many inland areas of Guangdong Province that are far from the provincial capital still mostly use silver. Recently, the Provincial Bank has sent personnel to purchase silver coins with additional 20% paper money (i.e., purchasing one yuan of silver coins with 1.2 yuan of paper money). Rural people are accustomed to the silver standard. For example, if they could buy 10 catties of local grain with one yuan in the past, they now need 1.2 yuan of paper money to buy 10 catties of grain. Thus, rice has become 20% more expensive invisibly. Considering the above reasons, the phenomenon of high rice prices has emerged recently. After learning about the reasons, the authorities, led by Governor Huang Musong, immediately telegraphed Li Zongren and Huang Xuchu of Guangxi Province, requesting them to lift the Guangxi rice ban to relieve the rice shortage in Guangdong Province. The telegram briefly stated that Guangxi Province has a surplus of grain, while we are constantly suffering from a shortage. At this time of harvest, we propose to adjust the surplus and make up for the deficiency, and order the lifting of the rice ban to continuously transport rice, which will be beneficial to the people's livelihood and economy of both provinces. It is said that Governor Huang Xuchu of Guangxi Province has other related issues to discuss regarding this matter, and plans to come to Guangdong during the day to discuss everything in detail with the authorities. As for the move by the Guangdong Finance Department and the banking sector to raise funds to purchase and transport Hunan rice, they are also actively raising funds. At the same time, in order to understand the production and sales of Hunan rice, the banking sector plans to form an investigation team to Hunan during the day to investigate in order to release loans for purchasing rice and continuously transport it to Guangdong.

Sixth Shanghai-Nanjing Express Derailed at Lingkou Station Yesterday Morning, Colliding with the Rear End of a Freight Train Parked at the Station: Fortunately, Passengers Were Safe, But Suffered a Fright 78

The sixth night express train from Shanghai to Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, which departed from Shanghai on the evening of the 17th, collided with the rear end of freight train No. 402 parked there when it entered Lingkou Station (Danyang 9.41 km), 202.69 km from the North Station, at about 4:00 AM yesterday (18th), causing two of the night express train's front wheels to derail. After receiving the report, the Railway Administration immediately dispatched a rescue train to try to put the front wheels back on the rails. It then continued its journey at 10:00 AM yesterday morning. Fortunately, all the passengers were safe, but they suffered a fright.

The 302nd Shanghai-Pingtou 2nd and 3rd class combined transport express train, which departed from the North Station at 12:00 PM on the evening of the 17th, stopped at Wujin Station at 4:00 AM yesterday (18th) after receiving the derailment report from Lingkou, as traffic was blocked. Subsequently, after the Railway Administration dispatched a rescue train to put the two derailed front wheels back on the rails, the sixth night express train continued its journey, and the 302nd Shanghai-Ping express train also followed.

Xiao Weiguo, Director of the Traffic Department of the two Railway Administrations, Chen Encheng, Deputy Director of the Engineering Department, and Gan Bi, Director of the Locomotive Department, took the fourth Shanghai-Nanjing 1st, 2nd and 3rd class express train to Lingkou Station from the Shanghai North Station at 8:00 AM yesterday (18th) to investigate, and prepared a report on the rescue process after the collision. They returned to Shanghai at 10:04 PM that night.

Jiangsu Province Handles River Dredging by Conscripting Labor: Total Mobilization Throughout the Province on a Fixed Date 79

Engineering Plans of Various Counties Approved, Actively Preparing: Starting Next Month, Building Dams and Pumping Water; Starting Work in February

Zhenjiang correspondence: The Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department is actively promoting water conservancy construction in the province. River dredging in various county villages is uniformly handled by conscripting labor. In urban areas, the method of drawing labor from able-bodied men is adopted. Now that the agricultural off-season has arrived, various counties have successively started work. The implementation of labor conscription for river dredging in this province this year is recorded below.

Various Counties Actively Planning Projects

Labor conscription in this province is mainly for water conservancy, supplemented by highway construction and afforestation. The Construction Department, considering that the period for labor conscription is imminent, previously ordered various counties to prepare. Currently, the projects to be undertaken by various counties, as well as the estimated project situation, the required engineering costs, and the benefited farmland, have all been investigated and completed. The labor conscription engineering plans and budgets of various counties have been approved separately, and the counties have been ordered to follow the approved plans and schedule the construction dates. The districts have been ordered to prepare according to the schedule. Regarding the engineering plans, the Construction Department has ordered the counties that have submitted their plans to the department to quickly prepare plans for review.

Total Mobilization and Work in February Throughout the Province

Chairman Chen of the province attaches great importance to this matter of labor conscription in the province. Therefore, the Construction Department must carefully select projects, prioritizing those that have a vital interest to the local people. Currently, various counties have dispatched technicians to assist in various districts, responsible for allocating work sections (allocating them based on proximity to their residences), urging the conscription of laborers, providing technical guidance, and inspecting and accepting upon completion. Regarding the dredging of main river projects, it has been decided that various counties will begin building dams and pumping water in January of next year. In February, all laborers conscripted in the province will be mobilized to start work, and it is stipulated that all work must be completed by the end of April, and submitted for review and acceptance at any time.

Using Baojia System to Organize Conscripted Labor

As for the methods of labor conscription, they fully utilize the baojia system for conscription. The method should be based on the bao as the unit. For example, when a certain bao is assigned work on a certain day, all households in each jia of the bao must go to work, so that the township, town, and baojia chiefs are jointly responsible for management and supervision. Furthermore, the department believes that the people of various counties may not have a deep understanding of labor conscription, and they should take the opportunity to instill knowledge about labor conscription during civic training and promote its meaning and effectiveness. The counties have been ordered to follow these instructions.

Songjiang 80

A Large Number of Suspects Escorted to the Province

The Third Security Command of Jiangsu Province has accepted a total of 16 suspects of endangering the Republic of China, presented by various counties, namely: Seng Guoyuan, Fa Jing, Xu Wenjing, Hong Jingshui, Sang Yebin, Zhu Jisheng, Chen Youxin, Jin Liusheng, Xu Leipei, Yi Wentong, Chen Qirong, Jin Zhongming, Xiang Juchen, Lin Genmiao, Xi Dafu, and Ding Yiyuan. After repeated interrogation, they were recorded and submitted to the province for review and instructions. Upon receiving orders to escort them to the province for interrogation, the Security Command ordered the 12th Security Battalion to send troops to escort the convicts along with the documents and items. After receiving the order, the battalion dispatched the platoon leader of the first company, Cai Jingqu, with eight soldiers, to escort them onto the train at 2:00 PM today to the province.

Prison Official Arrested After Leaving Office

Hou Qixiang, the former prison administrator of this county, was dismissed for repeated prison escapes and for finding opium being smoked by prisoners. Before the handover, he allowed 13 prisoners (outside workers) to drink in the downtown area in groups. After the county magistrate learned about it, he considered him to be perfunctory in his duties and suspected of dereliction of duty. After the official handed over his duties yesterday, he was sent to the local court's prosecutor's office for investigation. After being notified, he was escorted in person and scheduled for another interrogation.

Kunshan 81

All Circles Telegraph Requesting to Punish Zhang

All circles in this county are extremely indignant at Zhang Xueliang's treasonous rebellion. On the 17th, they jointly telegraphed the Central National Government and other authorities, requesting them to immediately order a punitive expedition, eliminate the traitors and rebels, and consolidate the national foundation.

Bandits Rob Peasant Households

The household of Jia Chief Zhu Renlong of the 5th Bao of Xiemaqiao in the 4th district of the county was suddenly visited by five or six bandits armed with weapons at about 11:00 PM on the 16th. They ransacked the house, taking away more than 300 yuan in cash and valuables. The next morning, a report was made to the county to pursue and arrest them.

Gaoyou 82

Soldiers and Bandits Engage in Fierce Battle, Rescuing Hostage

Soldiers of the 2nd Company, 1st Platoon, of the 23rd Security Battalion stationed in Jinkou Township, 2nd District, encountered bandits carrying a hostage on the 14th, who also attempted to rob the area. The soldiers immediately launched a fierce suppression. The bandits stubbornly resisted, and both sides opened fire. After a fierce battle for a long time, they were finally driven away, dropping a hostage. The bandits all fled for their lives. Fang Chongben and other local villagers sent 30 yuan in consolation.

Nantong 83

Mobilizing and Training Security Teams

The Fourth District Security Command has, starting from the 17th, mobilized security teams from various counties under its jurisdiction to Xiaoying in Tongcheng for training. The first phase includes one company each from Nantong, Rugao, and Haimen, and one detachment each from Jiang, Qidong, and Chongming, all combined into one battalion, with Zhang Weiqun appointed as the battalion commander.

Expanding the Opium Addict Factory

The Nantong District Opium Addict Factory is expanding its internal operations due to the increasing number of opium addicts sent from various counties for vocational training. Currently, the uniforms for the security teams in various counties under the district are all manufactured by this factory, and the quality is excellent.

Haizhou 84

Gathering to Discuss Anti-Drug Measures

The First District Public Office in this county convened dozens of county and township Baojia chiefs at 3 PM yesterday in the office's conference room to hold an anti-drug meeting. The meeting concluded that anti-drug policies are strict, and with the deadline for voluntary surrender approaching, the Baojia chiefs were urged to persuade opium addicts to surrender or seek rehabilitation as soon as possible, and not to test the law and face severe punishment.

Telegraphic Request to Punish Zhang Xueliang

The Xi'an Incident has aroused national indignation. The faculty and students of the Provincial Canal Rural Teachers School are extremely indignant. Yesterday, they telegraphed the central government and all sectors to punish the rebellious Zhang Xueliiang to uphold justice. The telegram reads: To the Shanghai Newspaper Association, forwarded to the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, the Military Commission, all institutions, schools, and newspapers: Reports state that the rebellious Zhang Biliang has telegraphed a rebellion, surrounding and detaining President Chiang. At this critical moment for the survival of the nation, the rebel dares to shake the foundation of the country. All those with blood in their veins are filled with anger. Therefore, we urge the central government to promptly punish him to maintain discipline, and call on all compatriots to condemn him unanimously and vow to eliminate this bandit. We are filled with urgent anticipation.

Shaoxing 85

Establishment of Granary Management

In order to promote the important policy of grain storage, the Shaoxing County Government has established a Granary Management Committee to manage the collection, storage, and management of grain throughout the county, in accordance with the provincial guidelines on grain storage.賀揚雲, 鍾家洲, 劉能趨, and twenty others have been appointed as committee members, and the committee is scheduled to be established on the 19th.

Hangzhou 86

Daily Rise in Food Prices

The price of rice sold in Hangzhou has recently risen sharply due to neighboring provinces such as Jiangsu, Anhui, and Jiangxi banning the export of rice, leading to a shortage of supply from Hushui. Rice merchants are suffering significant losses and have requested the municipal government to allow price increases. Yesterday, the rice price assessment meeting decided to increase the price of first to fourth grade fine rice and fragrant glutinous late rice by two jiao per dan, and fifth grade fine rice, secondary rice, and high-grade steamed rice by four jiao per dan, effective from the 17th. However, the price of rice is still expected to continue to rise, and the municipal government is working to increase supply.

Ningbo 87

Collapse of Building Injures Onlookers Watching the Bride

Zhou Asan, a resident of 205 Hutong Lane in this city, had his daughter Xiu Liao married on the 16th. Due to superstitious beliefs, the departure of the bride in the sedan chair was intentionally delayed. The sedan chair from the groom's family had been waiting for a long time, and the wedding matron repeatedly urged the bride to get ready. Many onlookers gathered upstairs, making a lot of noise. Unexpectedly, the floorboards and railings could not bear the weight and suddenly collapsed, causing all the men and women upstairs to fall down. More than ten people were injured, with Zhou Asan suffering the most serious injuries. The bride was also slightly injured. She hurriedly got into the sedan chair, and the event ended in disappointment.

Arrest of Suspected Traitor

Lin Jianzhong, a supervisory committee member of the Yinxian County Party Headquarters, arrested a suspected traitor, Lü Chisheng, at the Yongyigong Inn on the north bank of the river in this city on the 13th. He was handed over to the Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Jiaxing 88

Civic Assembly Condemns Zhang

Since the Xi'an Incident occurred, all sectors of Jiaxing have telegraphed Zhang Xueliang to persuade him to quickly realize his mistakes. At 9 AM on the 18th, a civic assembly was held at the sports field, attended by 4,000 to 5,000 people from various organizations, institutions, schools, militia teams, and the general public. After speeches by various representatives, the final resolution was to telegraph the central government to punish Zhang. Representatives were also selected from the militia teams and various organizations to go to the central government and Xi'an to petition the authorities to find ways to escort President Chiang back to Nanjing, preside over the political situation, unite against external enemies, and overcome difficulties together.

Cixi 89

Surveying Du and Bai Lakes

The Cixi County Government has decided to dredge Du and Bai Lakes in order to improve water conservancy in northern Cixi, and has submitted a report to the Construction Department for approval. Yesterday, a special commissioner was appointed to start with surveying by the end of this month, and thousands of reports have been printed and distributed to notify residents to assist in order to complete the water conservancy project as soon as possible.

Tokyo Correspondence

After the Stalled Sino-Japanese Negotiations: Japan's New Understanding of Diplomacy Towards China 90

— Nagumo

(I)

At noon on December 10th, the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs once again issued a "Declaration on China Policy." The main contents of this declaration are:

(1) Emphasizing the unshakable "China Policy" of the Empire.

(2) Deciding on the supreme principle of protecting the lives and property of Japanese people in China.

(3) Regarding past negotiations, listing various facts that the Chinese government has already "internally approved," refuting the Chinese side's claim of disagreement between China and Japan.

What we can see are only the texts published in Japanese newspapers, so we can only speculate based on the records of various Japanese newspapers.

According to the Tokyo Yomiuri Shimbun, the "agreement between China and Japan" mentioned by the Japanese side refers to the consensus on issues such as "tariff reduction," "hiring Japanese advisors," "Sino-Japanese transportation and communication," and "suppression of anti-Japanese activities." (The Chinese side's claims of disagreement are not discussed because the purpose of this article is to focus on the Japanese side.) However, since Japan claims that there is agreement, then the so-called issues on which agreement has already been reached have naturally lost their problematic nature. What should be paid attention to now is how Japan will force China to implement them in the future. The issue of how to force implementation is the serious issue for the future.

The supreme principle of protecting the lives and property of Japanese people in China is the "power politics" of "exercising military force." The Japanese Three Ministers' Conference (Minister of the Army Terauchi, Minister of the Navy Nagano, and Minister of Foreign Affairs Arita) issued the following conclusion: "Regarding the fundamental policy of protecting Japanese interests and Japanese people in China, we can only rely on the military force of the Empire. … The landing of the Imperial Navy Marine Corps in Qingdao this time is one example of precautionary measures. … Future policy towards China will undergo a major transformation, sweeping away the passive attitude of the past and turning to an active policy. …" This conclusion is already very clear and does not require further evaluation by the Chinese people. The dispatch of troops to Qingdao is certainly one example. The statement by the puppet state of Manchukuo on December 6th to support the Inner Mongolian army is also one example. Such examples can be seen at any time in the future.

As for the so-called imperial China policy, that has always been unshakable, and is now merely being emphasized again. What is the China policy? That is the well-known "continental policy."

(II)

During the three months of Sino-Japanese negotiations, every time a wave of bargaining occurred, the Japanese military immediately expressed a "tough stance" and a "major decision," as if the East Asian powder keg was about to explode. This powder keg is controlled by the Japanese military. Why is it that to this day, they are still only firing cannons outside the powder keg? Is it because the continental policy has been shaken? No! The Japanese ruling class understands very well that bullets and gunpowder cost money, and even becoming a victorious country will inevitably involve some sacrifices. If they can obtain actual benefits simply by intimidating, then it is most convenient to use cannons to intimidate diplomats. Manchuria has been conquered for five years, but they still have to sacrifice a great deal of Japanese wealth and lives for the few remaining volunteer armies. Conquering all of China would involve an even greater sacrifice, so they must be very cautious.

This caution is not about whether the powder keg should explode, but about the timing of the explosion. The decision on the timing of this explosion depends on Japan's current international environment and Japan's domestic situation.

Japan's current international environment, since the publication of the "German-Japanese Agreement," has clearly undergone the following changes:

(1) Japan has openly declared its participation in the international anti-communist front. Undoubtedly, the future confrontation between Japan and Russia will become even more acute. The European anti-communist front is led by Mussolini and Hitler. Today, the anti-communist forces that these German-Italian leaders can lead include Austria, Hungary, and the Spanish rebels. Needless to say, that is the fascist international anti-communist front. At the same time, the anti-fascist international front led by Russia and France includes Czechoslovakia, Poland, and the Spanish People's Government. Japan is using Hitler and the forces in his camp to threaten the Soviet Union, so that the Soviet Union cannot but allocate more troops to defend its western border. In this way, it is very beneficial in terms of the plan to wage war against the Soviet Union. However, there is no certainty of defeating the Soviet Union at present. The main purpose is to contain the Soviet Union and at the same time complete the continental policy. In the process of completing the continental policy, they are also strengthening preparations for war against the Soviet Union. This preparation process makes Japan the most important link on the fascist front. But—

(2) Countries such as Britain and the United States are also mocking this link. This mockery naturally stems from the contradictions between imperialist countries. However, Japan's sense of diplomatic isolation has not been reduced by much as a result.

(3) Japan is eager to turn China into one of the links in its chain. However, the Chinese government has stated that "anti-communism is a domestic issue," indicating that it is unwilling to participate. At the same time, the Chinese national independence struggle movement is developing, which is precisely in direct opposition to Japan's continental policy. The realization of Japan's continental policy means that there will be no independence for the Chinese nation. The independence of the Chinese nation means that Japan's continental policy will not exist. This contradiction is much stronger than the contradictions between imperialist countries. Japan wants the Chinese government to participate in anti-communism, but cannot abandon its continental policy. If the Chinese government abandons the struggle for national independence, it will lose its qualification for national independence and freedom. This is enough to make the Japanese authorities rack their brains. Suppose the Chinese nation, in order to strive for its own independence and freedom, actually allies with the Soviet Union. If the power within China and the Soviet Union (even if the Soviet Union can only allocate one-half or one-third of its national power) unite to fight against Japan, how will Japan cope? This is the focus of Japan's painstaking anxiety.

From Hitler's speech, we know that Hitler is thinking of preventing the communist movement within Germany, and at the same time wants to seize the Ukrainian farm in the Soviet Union. What place does Japan want to take from the Soviet Union? Japan has not yet made such a speech. However, the "Manchukuo" of "Japan and Manchuria are inseparable" has been established for four years. The North China problem and so on are still causing trouble. Can China be willing to abandon the struggle for national independence merely to complete Japan's continental policy and merely for anti-communism? Is Hitler willing to fight to the death? These are all things that Japan must consider.

(To be continued)

Yu Qiaqing: Yesterday, He Expressed His Views on the Shaanxi Incident, Stating That President Chiang Should Be Freed First and Strive to Suppress Bandits to Atone for His Crimes 92

Yu Qiaqing expressed the following views on the recent Shaanxi Incident yesterday: Qiaqing has served the community for more than fifty years. When the country was undergoing great changes and the national system was changing, there were many extraordinary people who rose to prominence and established meritorious service. Qiaqing has never belonged to any party. In the past twenty years of the history of the Republic of China, every reform has been followed, and those who have high vision, resolute will, perseverance, and have contributed to the country are the four people Qiaqing admires most in his life: (1) President Sun, (2) Governor Chen, (3) Executive Duan, and (4) President Chiang. Among the four, President Chiang has been with him for the longest time, so his contribution is also the greatest. Those who do not know think that Qiaqing is close to Chiang because of his hometown friendship, but this is not the case. In fact, most of Qiaqing's contributions are related to national and people's livelihood policies, and he has never interfered in personal power. The facts are there, and I believe they are well-known to the people of the country. Now that the three gentlemen, Sun, Chen, and Duan, have passed away one after another, President Chiang is the only one who seeks the welfare of the country and glory for the nation. President Chiang has long served as commander-in-chief, enduring hardships and working hard. He is loved by the whole country. In recent years, based on the principles of pacifying the interior and resisting foreign aggression, the suppression of the communists is about to be completed, the political system has completed unification, national defense has achieved victory, and diplomacy has been appropriate. The foundation has been consolidated, and the nation will soon see a revival. At this time of national turning point, when the commander-in-chief is exhausted, how should our people wholeheartedly support him in order to achieve complete success? Unexpectedly, a bolt from the blue descended from the sky, and the Shaanxi Incident occurred. This is what all the people of our country are united in indignation and hatred. I think that our domestic and foreign affairs have been in a difficult situation for a long time. Fortunately, President Chiang's hard work and perseverance, without complaining, have gradually achieved the goals of pacifying the interior and resisting foreign aggression. His achievements have surpassed those of the past and present. This is recognized by both China and foreign countries, and is not a private word of Qiaqing's preference. Now that President Chiang has been kidnapped, all plans for the benefit of the country and the people will fail. I don't know what the intentions of those who presided over the Shaanxi Incident are. They should be abandoned by the people of the country. I hope they will quickly repent, first restore President Chiang's freedom, and then work hard to suppress the bandits in order to atone for their crimes. Otherwise, the future of the country is unthinkable, and the nation will be plunged into an irrecoverable situation. The culprits will be irreconcilable with the people of the country. Unite as one, respond calmly, and hope to return our only leader. I hope my compatriots will encourage each other.

Secretary of the Japanese Embassy, Shimizu, Visited Yang Hu Yesterday, Conveying His Deepest Condolences to President Chiang and Discussing Central Policies and Local Security 93

Mr. Shimizu, First Secretary of the Japanese Embassy, visited Yang Xiaotian, Commander of the Songhu Garrison, at Mr. Yang's residence on Huanlong Road at 4 PM yesterday. It is reported that Mr. Shimizu was ordered by Ambassador Kawagoe to convey his deepest condolences to President Chiang for his temporary stay in Xi'an, and inquired about future central policies, paying particular attention to the security of this city, and expressed that the Japanese financial community unanimously supports the stability of China's finance in Shanghai. Mr. Shimizu has been stationed in China for many years and has a long-standing friendship with Mr. Yang, so their conversation was unusually cordial. During the conversation, Mr. Shimizu expressed his sincere admiration for Mr. Yang's command of all military and police forces in the Songhu area and his heavy responsibility for local security. They talked for more than an hour before he took his leave. In addition to expressing his condolences to Mr. Shimizu for President Chiang and thanking him for supporting finance, Mr. Yang replied to Mr. Shimizu as follows: (1) The Xi'an Incident is indeed a great misfortune for our country, but the consolidation of the central government, the stability of all parts of the country, and the national finance are absolutely not affected by the slightest incident. (2) President Chiang's temporary stay in Xi'an is safe and sound, and it is a definite fact. I believe that no Chinese would dare to harm President Chiang, because President Chiang is warmly supported by the military and civilians of the country, and even the women and children of the country. Anyone who harms President Chiang will never be tolerated by the 400 million Chinese people. (3) Regarding the future central policy, it will completely continue the past government and President Chiang's consistent policy without any change. The central government has clearly announced this. (4) Regarding the current martial law in Songhu, the Songhu Garrison Command is implementing the central government's circular, which is a common feature of all provinces and cities in the country. However, the situation in Songhu is more complicated. This martial law pays special attention to: 1. Strictly preventing communist elements from taking the opportunity to cause trouble. 2. Preventing the public from taking collective actions due to their support for President Chiang, which would affect local peace. 3. Strictly preventing those who are unwilling to spread rumors and stir up trouble, and prevent incidents that hinder the harmony of friendly countries.

Shanghai's Finance is Very Stable 94

Since the Xi'an Incident occurred, the stock trading of the Shanghai Chinese Stock Exchange has been stabilized by the maintenance of various banks. Foreign exchange has been maintained by the Central, China, and Communications Banks, and the British HSBC Bank. The three banks continue to buy and sell without restrictions and handle them according to past foreign exchange policies. Therefore, although trading is brisk, the exchange rate is still the same as the standard rate, which is one shilling and two and a half pence for British currency and thirty US dollars for US currency. As for the Chinese banks and money houses, they are well-prepared and can cope with the current situation, so finance is very stable. The money industry's foreign exchange rate has remained between eight and nine points.

Wireless Communications between Shanghai and Shaanxi Disrupted Yesterday 100

According to transportation agencies, wired telegraph service between Shanghai and Xi'an was restored once on the afternoon of December 15 at 8:00 PM, but was disrupted again at 9:30 AM on the morning of December 16. As a result, telegraph services have been temporarily relayed via wireless to Hankou and other locations. However, due to the lack of direct wireless lines between Shanghai and Shaanxi, the transfer of telegraphs from Xi'an via Hankou and other locations was also disrupted from 4:30 PM yesterday. As a result, wireless communications between Shanghai and Xi'an have been completely suspended. A Reuters report from Shanghai on December 18 stated that communications between Shanghai and Central and Northern China have been severely affected by the Xi'an Incident. Since Zhang Xue Liang announced his rebellion, wired and wireless telegraphs to Xi'an, Lanzhou, Hankou, Beiping, and other locations have been extremely congested, with official telegrams accounting for the majority. As a result, news and private telegrams have been much slower than usual, and some locations have been completely disconnected, including Xi'an and Lanzhou. According to a Reuters correspondent in Hankou, no airmail has been received in the past two days. A correspondent in Beiping also stated that airmail from Shanghai takes 48 hours to arrive.

Current Situation Affects People's Food Supply 101

Rising Prices and Difficult Living Conditions

The price of food in Shanghai, such as rice and flour, has been rising for the past two months due to strong sales in the north. Recently, the price has been inflated due to speculation taking advantage of the situation. Rice has risen to 11.6 or 11.7 yuan, reaching a peak in price compared to the old measure. Flour has risen to 4.3 yuan, which is over twice as high as the lowest price. The price is likely to continue to rise. Small businesses that sell rice and flour are all affected. Oil has risen to 25.5 yuan per dan. Salt is 360-370 cash per jin. Vegetables are over 3 yuan per dan. The value of foreign currency has decreased, and one French currency yuan can only be exchanged for 280 copper coins, which is 40 copper coins for 10 silver coins. This is a decrease of 200 cash from the previous month, which makes it difficult for ordinary people to live.

Eurasia Plane Flew from Shanghai to Chengdu Yesterday 102

But Flights to Lanzhou and Baotou and Zheng Lan Both Suspended

The Eurasia Aviation Corporation, with the approval of the Ministry of Communications, has temporarily revised its flight plan in response to the Xi'an Incident: (1) Flights from Shanghai to Zhengzhou, then from Zhengzhou to Luoyang, Chengdu, and Kunming. (2) Flights from Beiping to Taiyuan and then to Zhengzhou. Flights to Lanzhou and Baotou, and Zhengzhou to Xian and then to Lanzhou are suspended. Yesterday was Friday. A Kex (Junkers) giant plane departed from Shanghai at 6:30 AM carrying mail and passengers and heading west. It arrived at Zhengzhou at 10:40 AM, passed through Luoyang, and arrived at Chengdu at 5:00 PM. It will depart from Chengdu at 8:00 AM this morning and arrive at Kunming at 11:30 AM.

Implement Labor Service

More Than 60,000 People Mobilized to Dredge Rivers and Build Dikes; Groundbreaking Ceremony Held This Morning at Gaoqiao Seaside Bathing Beach; Mayor Wu Personally Broke Ground 104

The Great Community News Agency reports that the city's citizen labor service preparations are now complete. It has been decided to hold the groundbreaking ceremony at 11:00 AM today at the seaside bathing beach in Gaoqiao District, Pudong. More than 60,000 able-bodied men throughout the city have been mobilized to dredge rivers and build dikes. Details of the situation are as follows:

Ceremony Program

(1) Play music; (2) Pay the highest respect to the Party, the Nation, and the portrait of the late Premier; (3) Listen respectfully to the late Premier's will; (4) Chairman's speech; (5) Report; (6) Speech; (7) Hold the groundbreaking ceremony; (8) Photography; (9) Play music; (10) Ceremony concludes. Mayor Wu will personally break ground. The Labor Service Committee has also invited various agencies and organizations to send representatives to participate in the ceremony.

River Dredging and Dike Construction

The winter labor service projects stipulated by the Labor Service Committee are as follows: (1) Wusong District: Dredge Zhangjianbang and Shengjia Hong; (2) Yinhang District: Dredge Yuanchang River and Goose Pool, construct the Qianjiabang dike; (3) Jiangwan District: Dredge Xietang; (4) Yinxiang District: Dredge the western section of Yangshupu Qiujiang; (5) Zhenru District: Dredge Mugang Port, Qiujiang, and Taopu; (6) Pusong District: Dredge the southern section of Shahe River and Shuangyang Port; (7) Caojing District: Dredge Shang'ao Pond; (8) Gaoqiao District: Dredge the southern section of Huangtong Port, Qingpu Port, and construct Dongtang in Xin Port; (9) Gaohang District: Dredge Hutang Hong, Xiantang Hong, Chunshupu, and Hengbang; (10) Luhang District: Dredge Zhujia Gou, construct the Majiabang dike in the 44th Map.

Mobilizing Able-Bodied Men

The allocation of able-bodied men from each district for this service is as follows: Wusong, 3463 men; Yinhang, 4855 men; Zhenru, 6757 men; Gaoqiao, 6287 men; Gaohang, 2825 men; Jiangwan, 6258 men; Luhang, 2400 men; Caojing, 7577 men; Yinxiang, 7597 men; Pusong, 12,374 men, totaling 60,343 men. Gaoqiao District will start work today. The remaining districts will continue to implement the project as soon as preparations are completed, without holding further ceremonies.

Message to the Citizens

To raise awareness among citizens, the committee specifically issued a message to the citizens, saying: "Dear citizens, modern nations are built on the foundation of group living. Modern society requires everyone to be able to labor, serve society, and seek the welfare of society. If individuals only care about their own food and warmth, are selfish and self-interested, and only think about their own glory and wealth, then society cannot move forward, public morality will decline, and the nation will never be rich and strong. Therefore, Chairman Chiang said, 'If we want to be modern citizens and succeed in modern undertakings, we must labor.' Our labor must be meaningful, which means that in addition to doing our own jobs well, we must also do things that are beneficial to the country and society. We must serve society and the nation, and then a new nation and society can be built. The meaning of labor service lies in everyone serving the local area, everyone having the obligation to serve the local area, and engaging in national economic construction. Implementing labor service is the most urgent way to carry out national economic construction and an important stage in moving towards a new society and a new nation. It has been two years since the New Life Movement was initiated. Within these two years, the New Life Movement has spread throughout the country, and its influence has revitalized social customs. At the same time, labor service has made us realize that it is the best way to build a new society and a new nation. Now, the newly built roads, newly opened rivers, and newly created forests in various places, if added up, are countless. So many new constructions are the result of labor service, and their direct and indirect promotion of social welfare and national economic construction is truly a great force. Shanghai is the center of everything in the country, with a large population and flourishing industries. However, the rural areas near the city still have a lot of work to be done, such as opening up rivers, building roads, and repairing dikes, which require the labor of citizens to build. Therefore, starting from now, we have decided to first mobilize male citizens between the ages of 18 and 40 in ten districts, including Gaoqiao, Gaohang, Luhang, Jiangwan, Zhenru, Yinxiang, Yinhang, Pusong, Wusong, and Caojing, to dredge the canals needed for social development. The methods of labor service have been announced, and the work plan has also been decided. Citizens probably still remember that two years ago, the city suffered a severe drought. Although the drought was due to a lack of rainfall, the main reason was that the rivers in various districts of the city were silted up, making irrigation inconvenient and affecting the harvest of agricultural products. If we could have managed water conservancy well at that time, the drought would not have been so severe. This shows that dredging rivers is a very important matter. Moreover, diligence and labor are a good virtue in life, and they can also promote physical health. We can find many examples of this in history, such as Tao Kan moving bricks. Therefore, we believe that everyone's labor service now is both promoting social construction and welfare, and it is also beneficial to ourselves. Dear citizens, let us unite, take up shovels and hoes, and work together to serve the country, society, and our own welfare, and strive forward!"

New Initiatives of Dasheng Copper Factory 111

Dasheng Copper Factory was established in the second year of the Republic of China, specializing in the production of various construction supplies, furniture, and copper sheets of various thicknesses, made of pure refined copper. The factory's manager, Mr. Ling Jiannan, and engineer, Mr. Ling Jianxi, studied in Europe and America, specializing in various steelmaking machinery. After returning to China, they founded the Dasheng Copper Factory in Guangzhou. In the beginning, the factory was only a small business, but later business developed. They established a site with the production of copper. The factory’s high quality goods have been greatly received by all sectors. Recently, new machines have been transported from Europe and America, and the factory's products have been greatly improved. In order to expand its business, a Renhe branch sales office has been established at No. 62 Lloyd Road in Shanghai. The factory is the first in China to manufacture copper products by itself. It is sincerely a pioneer in domestic goods, and is truly a leader in the country's goods industry.

Relief Funds for Suiyuan Soldiers Received on Behalf of This Newspaper Office 112

Yesterday (18th), this newspaper office received relief funds for soldiers in Suiyuan from the following sources: 332 yuan and 37 cents from the One-Day Income Movement Committee of the Dingyuan County Government (an additional 332 yuan and 37 cents was sent separately to the Bank of China as a One-Day Income donation, a separate receipt was issued; the total remitted amount was 664 yuan and 74 cents); 348 yuan and 10 cents from teachers and students of the Shanghai Private Qiming Girls' High School; 255 yuan and 23 cents from employees and workers of the Xinyu Textile Factory No. 1; 105 yuan and 97 cents from the Fengyang County Strong Team Training Corps No. 8 Donation Group of the Linhuaiguan Joint Guarantee Office; 44 yuan and 20 cents from all the staff of the Jian'ou Middle School in Fujian; 1 yuan and 44 cents from Yu Yanpeng of Xun County; 41 yuan and 70 cents from all soldiers of the Jian'an Patrol Ship of the Salt Affairs Inspection Office; 13 yuan and 61 cents from students Fu Jiwen, Xu Bangjie, Hu Songen, Chen Xialing, and Wang Shijie of Minzhi Middle School; 1 yuan each from Zhou Shunli and Lu Zunwang; 93 yuan and 10 cents from Xu Dexin and others of the Yancheng Huasheng Company; 5 yuan from Wu Wenruo; 33 yuan from the Tongde Alumni Association (including 1 yuan each from Ji Fen, Mei Fengying, Zhang Zejun, Zhang Hai Ren, Chen Wang Shanj, Yu Dawei, Cao Yongxin, Han Jiu, Chen Yingu, Chen Shijun, Weng Zhichang, Zeng Guangshu, He Yunhe, Jin Xiezhang, Fu Jiren, Ma Jing, Zhu Wenxiang, Liu Jiyuan, Cai Wenqi, Sun Zhiyun, Zhou Moqing, Zhu Renying, Zhao Pinlian, Sun Cuizheng, Cheng Qian, Zhu Baoliang, Bao Baichi, Shen Bosen, Zhang Xiuyu, Fan Shouyuan, Sha Guang, Lu Shifu, and Song Keshen); 50 cents from Wang Zhicheng; 2 yuan and 55 cents from colleagues of the Xiang Dayuan Hardware Store; 30 cents from Yun Yucheng; 5 yuan and 90 cents from the Class 1 students of Qixiu Girls' Middle School.

The total received on the 18th was 1,284 yuan and 97 cents in national currency. Together with previous receipts, the total received was 79,970 yuan and 98 cents. After deducting the 77,900 yuan previously remitted to Chairman Fu of Suiyuan, the remaining balance is 2,070 yuan and 98 cents.

Shanghai County Launches General Review of Opium Addicts 113

Shanghai County has launched a general review of opium addicts. The implementation measures are as follows: (1) These measures are formulated in accordance with Article 5 of the Jiangsu Province Opium Addict General Review Measures; (2) For the general review work, the county government will appoint special commissioners, together with the responsible personnel of the County Party Department and the County Anti-Opium Committee, to supervise and urge all levels of autonomous public security personnel to earnestly carry out the work in various districts and townships; (3) The general review will be conducted in the form of autonomous areas, divided into five districts, with each large district further divided into two small districts, with each small district covering four or five townships; (4) The personnel for the general review will be mainly composed of personnel from the county public security bureaus and autonomous personnel. During the general review period, the public security autonomous personnel in the district will be subject to the command and supervision of the responsible personnel sent by the county government and the County Party Department and County Anti-Opium Committee to earnestly carry out the work; (5) The general review period is one month. From January 1 to 5, each district, township, and household will conduct a self-review. The head of the township will report the review process to the head of the township; from the 6th to the 10th, the head of the township will, after receiving the report from each head of the township, complete the review before the 10th and report the review process to the head of the township; from the 11th to the 17th, the head of the township will, after receiving the report from each township in the district, immediately complete the review and report the situation to the district head. From the 18th to the 26th, the county government will go to the townships within the district to conduct random inspections and complete the review. After completing the review, each county will report the situation to the county government. From the 27th to February 1, the county government, the County Party Department, the County Anti-Opium Committee, and all staff of the office will go to the countryside to conduct random inspections or complete the review. After completing the review, each county will report the results to the county government. (6) The responsible supervisory personnel assigned to each district and township are as follows (omitted). (7) After the general review is completed, each township will post the "Notice to Household Heads" issued by the county government on the upper right side of the main door of each household and inform them of the meaning of the notice (the notice must be posted neatly and firmly, otherwise, those who violate it will be punished for neglecting their duties). (8) Each land paste shop and smoking establishment will be responsible for propaganda and reporting during the general review period. After the completion of the review, they will issue a certificate stating that there are no opium addicts within their jurisdiction (the form of the certificate will be determined separately). (9) After the completion of the general review, each public security bureau will conduct a re-review by the director of the public security bureau and the patrol officer, and must issue a certificate stating that there are no opium addicts within its jurisdiction (the form of the certificate will be determined separately). (10) Regarding the general review work of opium addicts, the household registration police stationed in each district should conduct a detailed investigation of each household and report at any time. After completion, a certificate stating that there are no opium addicts in the police district should be issued (the form of the certificate will be determined separately). (11) The principals, teachers, and senior students of schools at all levels in the county should also be responsible for propaganda and reporting during the general review. Students in secondary schools should persuade their parents and explain the dangers of opium and the true meaning of the general review.

Overseas Chinese in Sydney Greatly Contribute to Disaster Relief 114

Overseas Chinese in Sydney, Australia, are known for their patriotism. Whenever there are disasters in China, they enthusiastically donate. The China Foreign Famine Relief Association at No. 505 Henan Road in this city held disaster relief efforts for the Jianghuai River floods last year. The Chinese Consulate in Sydney has repeatedly received huge amounts of donations and remitted them to Shanghai for disaster relief. Last month, the China General Association in that area held a grand dance party at the 7th Annual Fellowship Meeting to help raise disaster relief funds for the association, in order to entertain their peers and increase interest. After deducting expenses, the remaining 97 pounds sterling, 13 shillings, and 2 pennies, equivalent to 1,616 yuan and 41 cents in national currency, was remitted on the previous day by Mr. Gao Ya Lie, President of the Association, to Mr. Maxwell, General Manager of the British Chamber of Commerce Changxing Foreign Company and member of the Disaster Relief Committee of the Relief Association, for transfer. The overseas Chinese care for the victims, which is very touching.

Red Swastika Society Relief Team Working in Xinghe War Zone 115

The Red Swastika Society Relief Teams No. 1, 3 and 2 are currently stationed in Jining for rescue. The Charhar branch relief team is in charge of work in the Datong area. The Suiyuan branch relief team is working in Bailingmiao. The No. 8 Joint Team is in charge of work in the Xinghe area. According to reports, in this battle, the Xinghe front line was most severely affected in the area around Daqingshan and the county's Huangyu Township Yaozigou, No. 16, and Wan Gou and other villages. The food in each village has been completely consumed, and many houses have been destroyed by bombing. The team leader, Liu Xizhen, led team members, doctors, and physicians, including Dong Junfeng, to visit each village to carry out rescue work, bury more than 200 corpses, and transport the injured militia captain, Zhao Jizhong, and more than ten wounded soldiers back to Xinghe County for treatment. A shelter was also established in the county town to accommodate more than a thousand women and children from the affected villages.

Shanghai's Foreign Trade in November: A Sharp Increase in Trade Deficit 117

Imports: 46,882,031 Yuan

Exports: 30,805,557 Yuan

Trade Deficit: 16,076,474 Yuan

According to yesterday's announcement by the Jianghai Customs regarding Shanghai's foreign trade in November, imports amounted to 46,882,031 yuan, exports to 30,805,557 yuan, totaling 77,687,588 yuan. The trade deficit was 16,076,474 yuan. Compared to October of this year, imports increased by 4.2 million yuan, exports increased by 475,000 yuan, and the trade deficit increased by 4,675,000 yuan. Compared to November of last year, imports increased by 10,339,000 yuan, exports increased by 464,000 yuan, and the trade deficit increased by 9,865,000 yuan. From January to November of this year, cumulative imports amounted to 510,125,138 yuan, exports to 326,735,026 yuan, the total trade volume was 836,860,164 yuan, and the trade deficit was 174,516,113 yuan. Compared to the same period last year, imports increased by 32,097,000 yuan, exports increased by 75,947,000 yuan, and the trade deficit decreased by 43,040,000 yuan.

Imported Goods

In November of this year, imported goods included: raw cotton cloth, 88,243 yuan; bleached and dyed cotton cloth, 643,914 yuan; printed cotton cloth, 25,223 yuan; assorted cotton cloth, 40,857 yuan; cotton and cotton yarn, 7,356,14 yuan; assorted cotton products, 54,305 yuan; hemp and hemp products, 780,151 yuan; wool and its products, 2,461,543 yuan; rayon and its products, 838,599 yuan; metals and ores, 6,012,232 yuan; machinery and tools, 2,272,206 yuan; vehicles and ships, 964,150 yuan; assorted metal products, 1,840,046 yuan; fish and seafood products, 1,003,71 yuan; canned food and animal products, 478,390 yuan; grains and flour, 374,240 yuan; fruits, seeds, and vegetables, 314,812 yuan; medicinal herbs and spices, 367,312 yuan; sugar, 590,299 yuan; wine and beverages, 87,104 yuan; tobacco, 1,868,773 yuan; chemical products and pharmaceuticals, 2,484,266 yuan; dyes and pigments, 2,211,1713 yuan; candles, soda, petroleum, fats, and glues, 4,181,164 yuan; books, maps, and wood pulp paper, 2,869,200 yuan; leather and other animal product, 202,986 yuan; timber, 1,052,748 yuan; bamboo, rattan, palm, and their products, 410,201 yuan; asphalt, lime, etc., 321,897 yuan; porcelain, glass, etc., 315,844 yuan; stone and clay products, 152,309 yuan; sundry goods, 7,865,669 yuan; totaling 46,882,031 yuan.

Exported Goods

In November of this year, exported goods included: animals and their products, 3,622,942 yuan; leather, etc., 1,057,083 yuan; fish and seafood products, 41,574 yuan; beans, 520,655 yuan; assorted grains and their products, 1,539,352 yuan; vegetable dyes, 68,267 yuan; fresh and dried fruits and preserved fruits, 74,452 yuan; medicinal herbs and spices, 314,011 yuan; oil, 4,496,444 yuan; seeds, 2,550,373 yuan; wine, 36,829 yuan; tea, 2,126,887 yuan; tobacco, 196,205 yuan; vegetables, 174,302 yuan; other plant products, 289,941 yuan; bamboo, 35,475 yuan; fuel, 9,405 yuan; rattan, 237 yuan; timber and its products, 80,841 yuan; paper, 72,582 yuan; woven textiles, 6,480,300 yuan; yarn, thread, and needlework, 2,716,979 yuan; cotton cloth, 1,517,666 yuan; other textiles, 5,287,778 yuan; ore and metal products, 788,081 yuan; glass and glass products, 19,075 yuan; stone, clay, sand, and products, 59,410 yuan; chemicals, 305,637 yuan; printed materials, 154,606 yuan; sundry goods, 1,064,068 yuan; totaling 30,805,557 yuan.

Gold and Silver Situation

The import and export of gold and silver in November of this year included the import of 25,125 customs taels of gold from Hong Kong, plus 36,000 yuan. There were no changes in gold and silver exports. From January to November, cumulative imports totaled 1,075,179 customs taels of gold, plus 1,751,175 yuan. Of this, 761,137 customs taels of gold plus 1,689 yuan were imported from the UK, 304,420 customs taels of gold plus 1,747,000 yuan were imported from Hong Kong, 5,193 customs taels of gold plus 4,489 yuan were imported from Japan, and 4,419 customs taels of gold were imported from India. Exports totaled 16,239,122 customs taels of gold, plus 1,153,548,832 yuan. Except for gold, which was shipped to the UK, silver was shipped to the US in the amount of 1,126,886,471 yuan, to Hong Kong in the amount of 36,000,000 yuan, to the UK in the amount of 663,961 yuan, and to Japan in the amount of 500 yuan.

First Aid Association: Training Committee Meeting Yesterday 118

The Shanghai First Aid Association held its third meeting of the Training Implementation Committee at 5 PM the day before yesterday. Attendees included Tang Luran, Xu Yefu (represented by Zhu Jintao), Zhu Xuefan (represented by Jiang Wenyu), Tong Xingyue (Man Yun), Pang Jingzhou, and Fan Shouyuan. The meeting was chaired by Jiang Wenyu, with Wang Kui Sheng as the recorder. First, the chairman reported on the recruitment situation of the self-organized training class and the progress of assisting the China Second Vocational Supplementary School and Nanjing Road Commercial Supplementary School in running training classes. Then, discussions began: (1) Regarding the opening date and management of the self-organized training class, it was resolved to first open one at He'an Elementary School on North Chengdu Road, and Dr. Pang Jingzhou was asked to be responsible for hiring teachers. The selected students will be notified by the association after the opening date is determined. (2) Regarding how to handle requests for subsidies from already registered training classes, it was resolved to subsidize the China Second Vocational Supplementary School and Nanjing Road Commercial Supplementary School with 50 yuan each, and Wang Man Yun and Wang Kui Sheng were asked to inspect them. (3) Regarding how to investigate unregistered training classes, it was resolved to send letters of inquiry from the association. (4) Regarding drafting an outline for moral talks, it was resolved to ask Dr. Pang Jingzhou and Fan Shouyuan to draft an outline for moral talks and common sense for the training class. In addition, the association's Drug Supply Committee has received about 130,000 first-aid kits donated by various pharmacies. Recently, pharmacies that pledged donations have been directly sending them to the Red Cross Society. The association received 992 pieces of winter clothing donated by the Zhongxi Pharmacy yesterday, which will be sent to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Anti-Banditry Comfort First Aid Association.

Anhui Northern China Farmers Bank: Need to Establish More Exchange Offices 119

National Federation of Commerce Appeals to the Ministry of Finance to Order Compliance

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating that it had received a cable from the Anyang County Chamber of Commerce in Anhui, stating: "Since the implementation of legal tender in this county, the most commonly used fractional currency is issued by the Central Bank and the China Farmers Bank. These fractional currencies mostly circulate in lower-class society and change hands several times a day. After being used for a long time, they are severely damaged. However, the Central Bank has a branch in Bengbu, making it easier to exchange damaged notes. However, the Farmers Bank has not established exchange offices in various counties in northern Anhui. The bank's fractional currency is becoming increasingly damaged. Disputes often arise in merchants' transactions. If this continues, the market will come to a standstill, and merchants will be in dire straits. The association has repeatedly requested relief from higher authorities, but nothing has been implemented to date. Your association leads the entire country and is responsible for maintaining the interests of its members when they encounter difficulties. Therefore, we are submitting four damaged fractional notes from the Farmers Bank and requesting your review and referral of a telegram to the Ministry of Finance, ordering the bank to quickly establish exchange offices or authorize the Anyang Office of the Anhui Local Bank to exchange them without restriction in order to maintain the currency system and stabilize the market. We await your urgent instructions." Upon receiving this, it is appropriate to cable the Ministry of Finance for verification and request approval to order the China Farmers Bank to comply. Broken notes attached. Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, respectfully."

Tobacco Leaf Guild: Requests Release of Detained Domestic Tobacco 120

Domestic Tobacco Mistaken for Flue-Cured Tobacco; Letter to the Tax Bureau Explains

The Zida Tobacco Leaf Company, located at Pu'an Lane, Yong'an Street, French Concession, Shanghai, previously sold 100 packages of domestic Champion tobacco to the Shunkang Tobacco Company in Wenzhou. The Shunkang Company is now reselling it to the Xindongxing Early Tobacco Shop in Wenzhou. While the transaction was in progress, Erxun, an inspector from the Wenzhou Tax Inspection Office, mistakenly identified it as flue-cured tobacco (i.e., domestic American-type tobacco) and intervened, ordering 15 packages of tobacco to be sent back to the Bank of China warehouse and prohibiting any movement. Although Shunkang Company presented all the certificates from the tax authorities, the inspectors still insisted that samples be sent to Shanghai for inspection, refusing to allow free sale. Shunkang Company pointed out that when the batch of Champion domestic tobacco was transported from Shanghai to Wenzhou, it had been inspected by various local tax bureaus and customs offices, confirming that it was domestic tobacco, and they held a domestic tobacco tax certificate as proof. The inspectors neither trusted the certificates issued by the tax bureau nor had the experience to immediately distinguish domestic tobacco from flue-cured tobacco, so they hastily ordered the tobacco to be stored in a warehouse and prohibited its sale. In this situation, the legitimate business of tobacco merchants lacks legal protection. It has been reported to the Zida Tobacco Leaf Company, which has sent a letter to the local Tobacco Leaf Guild, requesting the Ministry of Finance's Tax Bureau to order its release immediately and to prevent intentional obstruction in the future in order to reassure the tobacco industry. It is also known that the local Tobacco Leaf Guild has already sent a letter requesting its release.

Flying Class Scheduled for Graduation Exams 121

The China Flying Society's flying class, which began training in June of this year, has been following the primary flying curriculum of the Central Aviation School, training daily. All students have decided to fly solo, and have also practiced and become skilled in various aerial maneuvers. Yao Xijiu, the secretary-general of the society, and the instructors believe that the studies have been completed. Graduation exams have been scheduled to begin on the 21st of this month and have been reported to the Aviation Commission, which will send personnel to supervise the exams. On that day, the exams will begin at 9:00 AM at the Longhua Airport, both morning and afternoon. The exams are expected to be completed in two days. The central supervisors, as well as the president Wu Tiecheng and vice president Wang Xiaolai, are expected to personally supervise the exams. A total of 31 students will graduate this time, including one female student, Yang Yingxun. It is also rumored that after the exams, the society plans to have the graduates leave the society first and await the periodic issuance of diplomas. Furthermore, the society, which first established civil aviation education in the country, has only two training aircraft, with a total flight time of more than 800 hours. Training has not been suspended in any weather conditions. Not only have all the students been able to complete their studies, but the aircraft have also never suffered even minor damage. Its achievements are truly commendable.

Yangtze River Cargo Weighing Issue: Continued Discussion of Solutions 122

The Shanghai Yangtze River Six Companies planned to weigh goods shipped to various Yangtze River ports according to the example of measuring dimensions. Starting from the 15th of this month, goods measured by weight would be weighed in full, including the weight of the packaging. However, the shipping companies could add a 5% commission to compensate customs brokers. This matter has provoked opposition from various customs brokers, resulting in the postponement of implementation on the 15th and an announcement of a temporary delay for further discussion of solutions. However, the attitude of the customs brokers is very firm, insisting that there is no room for negotiation unless the proposal is cancelled. Yesterday, the Six Companies convened the customs brokers again to discuss solutions. The customs brokers nominated the chairman of their guild, Chen Panjun, and two others to represent them in a second round of discussions with the Six Companies. However, the customs brokers refused to compromise on their demands and would rather organize a united strike. The two sides were unable to reach an agreement during the on-site discussion, so the matter remains unresolved.

Municipal Council Employees: Oppose Salary Cuts 125

Employees Union Lodges Protest; Police Department Personnel Considering

According to the Continental News, the special committee of the Municipal Council Employees Union yesterday (the 17th) formally protested to Feixin Dun, Director-General of the Municipal Council, regarding the salary cuts. It is said that what they oppose is the 8% salary cut is of secondary concern, what they oppose most is the reduction of compensation for losses in pension remittances and the reduction of various subsidies. At the same time, personnel from the Police Department are also considering lodging a protest, but it is unlikely to be implemented immediately. The leaders of each police station met last night at the Police Officers' Club on the top floor of the Fuzhou Road General Police Station to discuss the matter for a long time. They also held a meeting on Thursday night. The Police Superintendent did not attend either meeting. The results of the meeting were not announced. It is said that the police personnel believe that they should receive better treatment than personnel from other departments in order to be fair, because their duties involve dangerous situations. In recent years, theft cases have frequently occurred in the concession. During arrests, bullets fly and lives are at stake. Even if they are not killed, they are often disabled by bullets.

Hou Zongtai Sues Zhu Xianghe: Intentional Defamation 126

Lawyer Hou Zongtai sued Zhu Xianghe of the Zhuyu Industry Guild at No. 25 Houjiahong Road in the District Court for spreading words and intentionally defaming him. The petition stated: "The plaintiff and the defendant are both shareholders and directors of Jingfeng Printing and Dyeing Co., Ltd., and the defendant is a director and assistant manager of the company. The factory was established on May 10, 1934, with a capital of 50,000 yuan. The defendant, acting dictatorially, entered into contracts with Tongfeng Company for operating Jingfeng Factory with advances, collecting a security deposit of 20,000 yuan, and presenting a bankruptcy announcement to the First Special District Court, without convening a board meeting in accordance with the company's articles of association. The plaintiff objected to it, but afterwards, the defendant still convened a shareholders' meeting in his own name, intending to force shareholders to ratify his illegal conduct. The plaintiff sacrificed 1,820 yuan in cash and 3,000 yuan in shares for the Jingfeng Company and suffered from unclear entanglements. Therefore, out of a sense of responsibility, he published a notice in the Minbao on November 17, stating the facts to clarify his responsibility. Unexpectedly, on the 15th, the defendant fabricated false statements and suddenly published a news advertisement in the Ten Large Businesses, spreading words that were insulting to the extreme, saying (1) Mr. (referring to the plaintiff) is a director and uses his qualifications as a lawyer to threaten illegally at every turn. He usually turns clouds into rain and creates discord within the company, instigating lawsuits. Mr. volunteered to represent the company in court, thereby seizing several thousand yuan in legal fees from the company. Mr. has been successful in his own plan. (2) Mr. seized 2,000 shares by taking advantage of an opportunity at the beginning of the company's establishment. (3) Xianghe has too little legal knowledge, so Mr. was able to profit from it through clever means. (4) If Mr. publishes a notice in a semi-classical and seemingly understandable but unclear style again, I will not respond, etc. However, the plaintiff has always been very distant from the Jingfeng personnel, so how could he have turned clouds into rain? And in the two civil and criminal cases brought by former manager Huang Shengchang against Chairman Xie Meisan, Xie entrusted the plaintiff with several cases with a public fee of only 750 yuan. How could there be thousands of yuan? At the beginning of the company's establishment, Huang Shengchang voluntarily allocated 2,000 shares out of 20,000 yuan as compensation. How could it be called seizing it by taking advantage of an opportunity? And he has never received a cent from Jingfeng. How could it be called profiting from it? The plaintiff has studied hard for ten years, and the defendant's reference to 'semi-classical and seemingly understandable but unclear' is clearly intentional slander. Please investigate," etc. Yesterday, Judge Shao held a hearing, but the defendant did not appear. Chen Zhongyin, lawyer, requested a postponement. The judge ordered the hearing to be rescheduled for the 23rd.

Journalists Association: General Meeting Tomorrow 127

Zhu Baoxia and Others to Perform Famous Operas

The Shanghai Journalists Association will hold its fifth autumn general meeting tomorrow (the 20th) at 4 PM at the Zhengyi Society on the 7th floor of the Continental Commercial Building. New Invention by the Chung Hwa Book Company: "Eight-Function Calendar Clock" 129

Price: $18.88 Each

The Chung Hwa Educational Equipment Manufacturing Plant, established by the Chung Hwa Book Company, launched its invented and manufactured month, day, week, hour clock last spring. It was granted a special patent by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and exempted from transit duties by the Ministry of Finance. All sectors actively purchased it, praising it incessantly. However, the manufactured product was a wall clock, relatively large in size, only suitable for hanging in halls. Now, the plant's engineer, Mr. Ruan Shunfa, to meet general needs, has specially created a table clock that can be placed on a desk. Furthermore, a thermometer and hygrometer are embedded in the clock face. Thus, with one such clock, seven records – day, month, week, hour, day/night, temperature, and humidity – can be automatically displayed on one clock. How simple is that! But with ordinary desk clocks, even a slight misalignment can cause them to stop. This clock has a newly invented, adjustable clock stand installed internally, so it doesn't have this problem. As the year is coming to an end and all sectors are planning to purchase calendars, if they can purchase this clock, then a calendar becomes unnecessary. Using this as a gift, since it's a new invention, the recipient will definitely feel doubly interested. It is reported that the company, for the sake of widespread use, is now generally offering a special price of only $18.88 per clock. Both the Shanghai distribution office and the Beijing-Hangzhou branch have displays and welcome visits.
