Stranded Ship at Honggaopo Removed: Xunhan Route Reopened; Water Level in the Upper Reaches Plummets; Hankou at 2 Feet 4 Inches 133

—Shipping Companies Deeply Worried About Disruption—

For days, the Yangtze River ships of various Shanghai companies have experienced delays in imports and exports, with some being delayed en route for as long as three or four days. Regular scheduled ships have all been disrupted. The reason is that the river water level has dropped dramatically. Each Yangtze River ship going upstream or downstream, loaded with goods from Hankou, cannot travel directly. Upstream ships arrive in Jiujiang and then use barges to transfer goods. Downstream ships can only wait in Jiujiang for Hankou goods to be transported by barges, then reloaded onto the ships before heading east. Because the water level in the Jiujiang to Hankou section is surprisingly low, and the number of shoals increases daily, the navigable channel has become increasingly narrow. Yangtze River ships traveling to and from the Xunhan section have basically been unable to navigate at night, and even daytime navigation is extremely difficult. Furthermore, one incident has disrupted the traffic of Yangtze River ships: a large civilian ship suddenly ran aground at Honggaopo of Flame Mountain (a dozen or so li below Wuxue), the shallowest and narrowest part of the waterway, starting on the 13th, blocking the river and cutting off the navigable channel. This prevented the Yangtze River ships of six companies from traveling upstream and downstream. Subsequently, the Jianghan Customs specifically dispatched a small tugboat to the location to drag the stranded civilian ship to clear the waterway. However, it could only be moved a few feet, enough for small ships to pass with difficulty, but larger ships could not pass. As a result, the Jiangshun ship of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company was delayed and disrupted. Originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 15th, it only arrived yesterday afternoon. Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, Nisshin, and Sanpei ships were also blocked, with delays of up to five days. Only yesterday did the Jianghan Customs send a telegram to Shanghai, stating that the civilian ship that had run aground and blocked the river at Honggaopo had been removed after repeated attempts, and the obstructed channel near Flame Mountain, which had been blocked for many days, was now safe for passage. The companies received the telegram and distributed it to the captains of the Yangtze River ships for their information. However, in recent days, the water level in the Jiujiang-Hankou section has fallen further. The water gauge in Hankou is only 0.73 meters, equivalent to 2 feet 4 inches, which is the new record for the lowest Yangtze River water level this year. Upon receiving the report, the six companies have been loading even less cargo onto the upstream Yangtze River ships departing from Shanghai since yesterday. Even goods bound for Zhenjiang and Wuhu cannot be loaded, leaving a limited tonnage specifically for direct transport to Xunhan. A lot of goods are piling up in Shanghai, and Yangtze River passengers are extremely anxious. The 20% increase in shallow water fees does not cover the cost of transshipment, resulting in even greater losses for the companies. Currently, the Yangtze River ships of the six companies cannot operate on schedule, as there are constant incidents of blockage and grounding. If the water level continues to drop, Yangtze River ships will truly be unable to pass through the upper reaches of the river.

Tuberculosis Exhibition Success 136

The Shanghai Tuberculosis Exhibition, which opened on the 15th at the Wuzhou Pharmacy, has been visited by thousands of people daily. The exhibition displays various models and specimens of tuberculosis, tuberculosis statistics, tuberculosis prevention photos, health books, etc., to promote public awareness and is indeed essential. The association recently noted that people from all walks of life are not fully aware of X-ray examinations. Therefore, it especially informs the public: (1) Anyone suspected of having lung disease, regardless of whether they have any pain or symptoms. (2) Anyone suffering from respiratory diseases for more than three weeks and not recovering. (3) Anyone who has frequently experienced respiratory diseases in recent years should undergo an X-ray examination. Summing up the above, a definite rule is that it is a mistake to determine that one's lungs are healthy without an X-ray examination. In other words, a doctor cannot determine that a patient has no lung disease without an X-ray examination. Therefore, for accurate diagnosis of lung health, an X-ray examination is essential, especially X-ray photography. It is known that the China Tuberculosis Association holds X-ray examinations every Monday, Wednesday, and Friday mornings at the First Clinic at 306 Fangxie Road, Ximen, and every Wednesday morning at the Hongqiao Sanatorium Branch at 2 Daxi Road. Anyone suspected of having tuberculosis should be examined as soon as possible to implement early diagnosis, which will be of great benefit to tuberculosis prevention work.

Bus Driver Kills Two People in Accidents: Sentenced to Two Years and Six Months Imprisonment; Appeals the Original Judgment 140

Zheng Changyou, a Dingbei native, age 33, a driver of British-owned China General Omnibus Company bus number 472, killed someone in a car accident in the Public Concession last year. He was sentenced to imprisonment by the First Special Court and given a suspended sentence. Before the suspension period was over, at noon on October 28 of this year, Zheng was driving public bus number 15089 and driving on Haige Road. When approaching the intersection of Zhaofeng Road and Maiqi Road, a Zhou Amao, an apprentice at the American fruit store in Jingansi Road, was riding a bicycle in front. The Zheng driver was careless, only honked the horn, and did not brake, but drove straight forward. Zhou heard the horn and misunderstood, dodging to the side of the road, and was hit by Zheng's bus, dragged for about three yards. Zhou's arms and ribs were broken and he died before medical treatment could be given. The French police detained Zheng and brought him to the Second Special Court for prosecution. Judge Sun Penghuai concluded the trial and recognized that Zheng was sentenced by the First Special Court, and the suspension period had not expired. He committed a negligent manslaughter again, and his circumstances were particularly heinous, so he should be punished severely. Zheng was sentenced to two years and six months imprisonment. Zheng Changyou appealed the judgment to the Third Branch of the High Court. Yesterday, Wu Tingqi, the presiding judge of the Criminal Court, together with judges Wang and Liao, and prosecutor Dong, attended the Criminal Court Three for questioning. Lawyer Fei Xizhen from the French Police Department appeared in court. The court first questioned the appellant's reasons for disagreeing with the original judgment and the details of the accident. Then, according to a report from the traffic office's western police officer on the investigation after the accident, the court also summoned witness Gu Jingduan, a Chinese police officer number 300 from the Jingansi Police Station, who witnessed the accident. The court ordered a rescheduling of the hearing, and the appellant was still returned to the detention center to await review.

Divorce Case Hearing: Cross Signature Examination Results Show Not Written by the Same Person; Remarriage Case Heard Again Yesterday 146

In the case of Zhuang Tinggui from Wuxi and his newly married wife Za Lili being sued for bigamy by Zhuang's divorced wife, Zhu Yundi, the First Special Court's Judge Qian Hongye held another hearing in the first criminal division yesterday morning. Zhuang's lawyer, Chen Tingrui, stated that he was instructed by the court to reconcile with Ms. Song. The defendant was willing to add a considerable sum to the alimony already given (over three thousand yuan). However, Zhu insisted on returning to the Zhuang family, resulting in the failure of reconciliation, etc. The court then immediately declared that the cross signature written by Zhu and the signature on the divorce document signed by Zhu had been sent to the Institute of Forensic Medicine for examination, and it was determined that they were not written by the same person. Subsequently, the court ordered the start of the debate. The police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, argued that in addition to the crime of bigamy, Zhuang had also committed the crime of forging documents and requested a judgment according to the law, etc. Lawyer Chen Tingrui argued that regarding the point of whether or not there was a divorce, this case already had testimonial and material evidence, etc., sufficient to prove that there was indeed a divorce. As for the signing of the cross, the person must be illiterate, so the signature today would be like this, and tomorrow another format, which is a common occurrence. Therefore, civil law stipulates that the signing of a cross must have two or more witnesses. Moreover, the circumstances under which Zhu signed the divorce document and when she came to court to write several clumsy crosses were completely different. The discrepancy in the signatures was a natural occurrence, and she should be declared innocent, etc. Judge Qian then instructed Zhu's lawyer, Wang Shizong, that this case should first file a civil suit to confirm that the divorce document was invalid and then adjourned the case for another hearing.

Missing Girl; Lawsuit for Disrupting Family 147

Chen Cai, a woman from Wuxi, is thirty-eight years old and resides in her hometown. In November of the eleventh year of the Republic (1922), because she had many children, she voluntarily gave her two-year-old daughter, Jin Di, to Guo A'liu (also known as Guo Mao), a woman from the same hometown who resided at 94 Xiangfen Lane, as an adopted daughter. Raised until now, Jin Di is now sixteen years old. In order to secure her future livelihood, Guo A'liu ordered Jin Di to learn dancing, so that she could rely on it for a living. Unexpectedly, on the 3rd of this month at around 8 PM, Jin Di suddenly pretended to go out shopping and never returned. Guo A'liu immediately published an advertisement the next day to search for her. On the 5th, Guo A'liu suddenly received a letter from lawyer Xu Jinyu, which stated, "According to Shen Yiqing, my sister, Jin Di, has recently been forced by Guo A'liu to engage in prostitution, soliciting customers everywhere. Forcing a good woman into prostitution is prohibited by law, but Guo A'liu is blinded by profit and has committed a crime. I have no choice but to take my sister back and give you three days to come and discuss a solution, otherwise I will pursue legal action," etc. After receiving the letter, Guo A'liu realized that her adopted daughter, Jin Di, had been seduced by Shen. She then sent a letter to her biological mother, Chen Cai, asking her to come to Shanghai and engage lawyer Zhu Honglie to file a lawsuit with the First Special Court against Shen Yiqing for disrupting the family, violating Articles 227 and 241 of the Criminal Law, and attaching a civil suit for compensation for mental distress of five hundred yuan. Yesterday afternoon, this case was heard by Judge Huang Risheng in the Eighth Criminal Division. Shen Yiqing did not appear, nor did a representative lawyer appear in court. After Judge Huang briefly questioned the plaintiff and others, he ordered the hearing to be postponed.

Fuan Amusement Park; Pregnant Woman Collapses Unconscious 148

After the Xiaoshijie Amusement Park in southern Shanghai was burned down, only the Fuan Amusement Park on Dongmen Road remained in operation, and as a result, there have been many visitors in recent days. Yesterday afternoon at 3 PM, a pregnant middle-aged woman, visibly advanced in her pregnancy, was pushed and suddenly collapsed unconscious. Her surname is unknown. She was taken to Nanyang Hospital by a police car.

Orphan Sent to the Bureau for Relief 149

Tang Zikang, a fourteen-year-old boy from Suzhou, resides at 64 Gushi Lane in Suzhou. His parents are deceased, and he depends on his aunt and uncle for survival. Recently, he was mistreated by his aunt and uncle and found it unbearable, so he secretly fled to Shanghai. However, he was unfamiliar with the place and had no one to take him in. Yesterday afternoon, he was crying at Lao Beimenxi on Minguo Road. Hu Yifeng, a fellow townsman living in Aijia Lane, saw him and asked why he was crying. The boy recounted the details of the mistreatment and his escape and recognized Hu as a compassionate person, willing to recognize Hu as his stepfather and asking to be adopted. Hu, however, was concerned that the boy's background was unclear, so he reported it to the police and took him to the police station, which transferred him to the bureau for relief.

Woman Abandoned by Lover after Divorce 150

Zhuang Zhuang, a forty-year-old woman from Suzhou, lives at 5 Huamei Lane, Zhangjia Lane in the city. She has only one daughter, Fengzhen (also known as Da Meimei), who is twenty years old and beautiful. She married Yao Zhongsheng a year ago. Unexpectedly, Fengzhen had a passionate affair with Lu Shoumin (twenty-four years old), an insurance agent living at 5 Wufu Lane, Xueyuan Road. Lu instigated Fengzhen to divorce her husband in order to live together as husband and wife. It went to court, and as a result, she compensated her husband seven hundred yuan for the divorce. Later, she repeatedly urged Lu to formally marry her, but he remained evasive. Recently, the two had conflicting opinions. Fengzhen demanded the return of the compensation money paid to her ex-husband, but Lu refused. Therefore, a few days ago in the afternoon, she dragged him to the Yi Miao Police Station, accusing Lu of being ungrateful and seductive and asking for the money to be recovered. After interrogation, it was found that the case was related to a marital dispute, which was a civil matter and should be sued in court.

Guiding Agency Child Steals While Distributing Flyers 151

Discovered, Leading to a Dispute; Sentenced to Detention with a Two-Year Reprieve

Zhang Jin (also known as Qin), an obstetrician from Changzhou, resides at 24 Weiwei Lane, Weihaiwei Road. The other day, because her relative, surnamed Zhou, was holding a celebration at the Yan Maoyuan Restaurant at 267 Hubei Road, she went to congratulate him. At the time, she placed her velvet vest in the cloakroom. That morning, two pieces of clothing were stolen from the cloakroom, so Zhang paid close attention. Unexpectedly, at 7 PM, while seating arrangements were underway, Ji Wentian, a fifteen-year-old child from Tongzhou who distributed flyers for the Tiansheng Guiding Agency at 305 Gongqing Building, 454 Hankou Road, came in, and under the pretext of distributing flyers, sneaked into the cloakroom and stole Zhang's velvet vest, attempting to escape. Zhang saw him and stopped him. Because he was young, she released him after a slight reprimand. Unexpectedly, the child returned to the agency and complained to the agency owner, Ms. Li Li (twenty-five years old, also known as Li Lili), a woman from Ningbo. She immediately led female guides Wu Jie and Zhang Wenying, and Ji Wentian, to Yan Maoyuan to reason with Zhang, making a loud commotion and intending to invite Zhang to a Yile Tian Teahouse to settle the matter (commonly known as "eating jiang cha"). Zhang firmly refused, leading to a continuous dispute. The Yan Maoyuan staff reported to Hua Constable Bao Tan and Cao Qishan of No. 3188, who arrested Ji Wentian and Li Li and took them to the Lao Zha Police Station. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Second Criminal Division of the First Special District Court. Police lawyer Qian Xunjiu explained the situation and prosecuted them for theft under Article 320 of the Criminal Law and for restricting freedom under Article 305 of the same law, requesting punishment according to the law. After Zhang Jin testified, Ji Wentian and Li Li denied the facts of theft and restricting freedom. After interrogation by Judge Ye Shengchao, Ji Wentian was sentenced to 20 days of detention for theft, with a two-year reprieve, and Li Li was acquitted.

Monks Repeatedly Frame and Extort 152

Yue Lai, the abbot of Lingshan Temple on Fushentang Street in the Nanshi, trusted Pu Huai, the temple's receptionist, because of his loyalty and competence. However, this caused jealousy among others. A few lawless individuals who had previously been dismissed colluded with a gangster named Gao and others. When their extortion failed, they secretly placed morphine and other drugs in Pu Huai's room and anonymously reported it to the police, who arrested him and sent him to the Shanghai Garrison Command. Fortunately, the investigation revealed that he had been framed, and he was released on bail. Recently, Abbot Yue Lai received three anonymous letters on the 16th, 20th, and 28th of last month, attacking Pu Huai and demanding his expulsion. Fearing further accidents, he presented a petition to the patrol lane police station requesting an investigation.

A Loud Bang; Zhang Huagen Injured 153

Zhang Huagen, a thirty-four-year-old man from Zhapei, Zhejiang, lives with his wife, Ms. Ni, and their three children at 2 Shunfa Lane behind the South Railway Station. Recently, Zhang, with the help of friends and relatives, collected some capital to manufacture toy firecrackers at home. Yesterday morning at 7 AM, Zhang placed the manufactured firecrackers on a table in the room. He carelessly turned on the light, and the light bulb exploded, accidentally touching the firecrackers. With a loud bang, the firecrackers on the table were completely detonated. In an instant, smoke filled the air, and Zhang's head, face, hands, and feet were injured. The Chenjiaqiao police station, upon hearing the news, dispatched police officers to investigate and found that the injured man's condition was quite critical. They immediately sent him to the Xin Puyu Tang Hospital for treatment and took Zhang's wife, Ms. Ni, to the Ximen branch for questioning before transferring her to the headquarters for further investigation.

Robbery on Rue du Consulat 154

The home of Zhu Wenli, a Ningbo native, at 14, Lane 516, Rue du Consulat, was robbed by three bandits yesterday afternoon at around 3 PM. Two of the bandits had pistols. After entering the house, they first held the men and women inside captive and then began to search and rob the house. In total, the bandits stole more than 500 yuan before fleeing. Afterward, the victim reported the incident to the French police and requested an investigation.

Weather Report 164

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that Shandong is cloudy and cold all around, with snowfall in several places, and strong hot northwest to northeast winds. The upper reaches of the Yangtze River are calm and windless. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River have strong north to northeast winds. The East Sea and Taiwan are cloudy and rainy, with strong north to northeast seasonal winds. Also, the highest temperature in this city in the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday was 48.7, and the lowest was 36.0. On the same day last year, the highest was 39.6, and the lowest was 28.9.

Ten-Foot Pearl Curtain

Chrysanthemums are abundant in late autumn and gradually become scarce in winter, so winter chrysanthemums are especially precious. Chrysanthemum lovers often regret their scarcity. The various chrysanthemum varieties produced by the Huang Family's Animal and Plant Breeding Farm in Zhenru have always been well-known. After many years of research and cultivation using scientific methods, they have obtained hundreds of pots of famous chrysanthemum varieties this year. As winter approaches, the owner of the Huang family, in order to share with everyone and avoid regrets, has specially entrusted the Wang Kai Photo Studio on Nanjing Road in this city to sell them at a very low price. Each pot is sold for only one yuan in national currency. With such a low price, such a valuable famous flower is an opportunity that chrysanthemum lovers should not miss. The picture above is named "Ten-Foot Pearl Curtain", a famous variety of the Huang family, published to give a glimpse.

Chinese Sports Federation Cross-Country; Date Decided 168

3:30 PM on the 23rd; 3,000 Meters Full Course at Hujiang

This year's Chinese Sports Federation cross-country race has been decided to be held at the Hujiang Affiliated Middle School in Yangshupu in this city before Christmas. According to the registration results, the participants include Fudan Shizhong, Fudan Affiliated Middle School, Private Shangzhong, Guanghua Affiliated Middle School, and Hujiang Affiliated Middle School. It is reported that the cross-country running committee of the association convened a meeting yesterday and decided on the following key issues:

(1) Date: Set for 3:30 PM on the 23rd of this month, to be held near Hujiang Affiliated Middle School in Yangshupu.

(2) Units: The schools participating in this year's event include Fudan Shizhong, Fudan Affiliated Middle School, Private Shangzhong, Guanghua Affiliated Middle School, and Hujiang Affiliated Middle School.

(3) Distance: A total of 3,000 meters.

(4) Route: Starting from the front of the Hujiang Affiliated Middle School gate, heading north on Jungong Road to the Qiujiang Bridge, turning back, and returning along the original road to the starting point at the front of the Hujiang Affiliated Middle School gate, for a total of 3,000 meters.

(5) Scoring: The order reciprocal scoring method is adopted, that is, the first place gets one point, the second place gets two points, and so on. Each school is limited to the six athletes who arrive first.

(6) Championship: The school with the lowest total score wins the championship. However, if each unit has fewer than six people attending, no points will be counted.

(7) Referee: Hired by the committee.

(8) Number Cloth: To be collected from the Hujiang Sports Department one hour before the race. Pins must be self-provided. Each athlete will receive two number cloths, which will be pinned on the front chest and vest. All four corners must be pinned firmly, otherwise participation will not be allowed.

Starting at 8 AM in Hongkou Park, with a Total of 123 Participants

The 20,000-meter long-distance race organized by the Hongkou Cross-Country Team is scheduled to start at 8 AM tomorrow morning at the west entrance of Hongkou Park. Race numbers will be distributed on-site half an hour before the race tomorrow. Details are as follows:

Route

Starting from Xiamen Road at Hongkou Park, proceeding along Jiangwan Road, then along West Sports Association Road, Xiangyin Road, crossing the Xiangyin Road wooden bridge, turning into Jungong Road, turning left onto Wuquan Road, passing in front of the Municipal Government and Sanmin Road, turning left onto Songhu Road, then turning right to reach Xiangyin Road, heading straight to West Sports Association Road, via Jiangwan Road, entering the west entrance of Hongkou Park, finishing in front of the flower hall.

Important Information

Jiangsu Department of Education Experts: Examination of the Performance of Students in Private Schools 179

Ten Measures Promulgated and Implemented, Orders Issued to Education Bureaus in Various Counties to Comply

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, in order to assess the teaching performance of private schools in various counties and to enhance the effectiveness of promoting compulsory education, has specially formulated provisional measures for examining the performance of students in private schools, and has issued a notice to the education bureaus of various counties to comply with them. The news was reported in yesterday's newspaper. The details of the measures are as follows:

(1) The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education has specially formulated these measures in order to assess the teaching performance of private schools in various counties and to enhance the effectiveness of promoting compulsory education. (2) At the end of each semester, the education bureaus or county governments of each county shall conduct a county-wide student examination in private schools, either by district or centrally. (3) The subjects of the examination are Chinese language, arithmetic, and general knowledge. The level of the examination for each subject is based on the graduation standards of primary schools. (4) The examinees shall be limited to purely private school students. Those who have graduated from elementary schools or are currently studying in elementary schools shall not be allowed to take the test. (5) Before the examination, the education bureaus or county governments of each county shall order the private schools to submit a list of the names, native places, ages, and genders of the students taking the examination to the education bureaus or county governments for verification. (6) The question setting and grading shall be presided over by the education bureau or county government. (7) Students who pass the examination shall be issued a certificate of completion of compulsory education by the education bureau or county government. (8) Students who have passed the examination and have obtained a certificate of completion of compulsory education shall not be allowed to take the examination again. (9) If the examination results of the students in each school are excellent, the education bureau or county government may grant the teacher of the school a certificate of merit or a bonus, depending on the grade. Those with excessively poor results will be banned. (10) These measures shall be promulgated and implemented by the Department of Education and submitted to the Ministry of Education and the Provincial Government for record.

Shanghai Boy Scout Wartime Service Corps to Begin Registration Soon 181

Headquarters Temporarily Located in the Boy Scout Council

The Shanghai Boy Scout Wartime Service Corps, initiated and organized by the Shanghai Boy Scout Council, has attracted many young people who have come to inquire about the details since its preparation. It is learned that the organization regulations of the corps have been drafted and the personnel have been nominated. The organization is divided into eight major teams: engineering, transportation, communication, reconnaissance, rescue guidance, recruitment, and special affairs. The training includes military police, reconnaissance, air defense, rescue, anti-poison, and engineering knowledge and skills. The training of the corps during peacetime is based on the principle of not hindering the school curriculum of the members. Mobilization and departure when necessary will not be restricted by this. Outstanding young people in this city who are at least 16 years old and have received secondary education may register, but they must be investigated and reviewed before being allowed to join the corps for training. It is learned that the corps is scheduled to begin registration on the 22nd of this month (Tuesday). The headquarters is temporarily located in the Boy Scout Council at Daji Road, Ximen.

Xinhua Art Academy Held Its 10th Anniversary Ceremony Yesterday 182

Exhibition Held at the Same Time; Thousands of Male and Female Guests Attended

Xinhua Art Academy in this city has been established for ten years. Yesterday was the school's tenth anniversary celebration. The celebration ceremony was held at 10:00 AM, and a commemorative exhibition was held at the same time. Representatives from Party and government agencies and about 1,000 male and female guests attended. The ceremony was solemn and grand. The ceremony venue was set up in the school's research room. A colorful arch was erected at the school gate, and the Party and national flags were hung. Teachers of the school stood respectfully at the entrance to welcome guests. Students were also stationed at the entrance of the auditorium and on both sides of the road to welcome guests and maintain order. Guests from all walks of life entered the venue one after another. The hall was spacious and elegant. The congratulatory inscriptions and mirror screens presented by various parties around the hall were dazzling and beautiful. The Party and national flags were hung on the chairman's platform. The ceremony began in the midst of melodious and orderly songs, and was serious and solemn. After the music, the school's dean of studies, Zai Yachen, delivered the opening speech, reporting on the progress since the establishment of the school. Then, Party and government officials delivered speeches, and guests spoke. First, He Bingsong, the current president of Jinan University, delivered a speech on behalf of the Minister of Education, saying that the true meaning of art is truth, goodness, and beauty, and that the study of art must pay attention to harmony and perspective. Then, Mayor Wu's representative, Li Dachao, delivered a speech, saying that he hoped that the colleagues of the school would maintain their spirit of hard work, maintain their past history, and continue to work hard to carry it forward. Then, Director Pan of the Social Bureau delivered a speech, saying that the study of art should be integrated with life and fused with the national character. Then, Principal Jiao of Liming delivered a speech on behalf of the Shanghai University Federation and the China-Soviet Cultural Association, saying that people should have six educations in the world, namely moral, intellectual, physical, social, aesthetic, and skill, and aesthetic education should be used to run through them. From this, we can know the importance of aesthetic education. Finally, the founders of the school, Yu Jifan and Pan Boying, gave speeches, and Wang Yachen delivered a reply. After the ceremony, guests and faculty took pictures and dispersed. Director Wang accompanied the guests to visit the newly established carpentry workshop and the achievement exhibition. In the afternoon, a Western music concert, a recreation meeting, and a Xiao Shao Orchestra Chinese music performance were held at the Chinese Arts and Crafts Society on Emmet Road.

Fudan University Saves Coal to Aid Suiyuan 185

Fudan University has implemented measures to save coal and contribute to Suiyuan starting this week. All offices in the school will not be heated this quarter. Heating will only be provided if the weather is cold enough for the Fahrenheit thermometer to drop below 40 degrees, causing water to freeze and hindering writing. The library and reading room will also only be heated if the temperature drops below 40 degrees. The hygiene team's examination room and other special circumstances may be determined according to the climate. All faculty, staff, and student dormitories will also not be heated. If faculty members want to install their own stoves, they must pay 20 yuan per person per month for coal, with the surplus used as a donation to aid Suiyuan.

Market Moving Towards Normalcy, Cotton Yarn, Cotton, Grains, Flour and Wheat All Falling, Government Bonds See Rise, Exchange Rates Strengthen 186

Yesterday's market gradually returned to normalcy, sweeping away the anxiety and apprehension of the past few days. Consequently, bullish cotton yarn traders were already selling off their positions. Although prompt delivery prices remained firm, forward delivery prices fell by more than five yuan. Cotton also shifted from buying to selling. In the minds of speculators, there was no longer any concern about currency prices. Even yesterday's foreign exchange market, although English and American tobacco companies were settling transactions in shillings, Chinese merchants were actively reselling their previously acquired holdings, causing exchange rates to strengthen. This is a reflection of financial stability. Bullion buying was also subdued. The government bond market, which often takes politics as its backdrop, saw a rise in all unified bonds yesterday. Ding bonds saw the largest increase, rising by one yuan and nine jiao. December C bonds also rose by one yuan and seven jiao and five fen. Other bonds rose by one yuan and three or four jiao. Flour prices, which had been rising wildly for days, continued to rise in the morning for each month's contract, ranging from two fen to two fen and seventy-five per cent. However, in the afternoon, as the situation unfolded, flour prices in the later market fell more than they rose, down by four or five fen compared to the morning. Wheat prices fell by one jiao in the afternoon. The impact of Jiang Dingwen's return to Beijing on the Shanghai market was like the weather yesterday: overcast and gloomy in the morning, threatening snow, but by noon, the sun was shining brightly.

Yarn Flowers: Actual Sales Ultimately Lackluster; Cotton Yarn Marked by Heavy Selling; Distant Futures Plummet by a Steep Five Yuan; Current Month's Decline Still Slight 187

The yarn market is trending weak, and the decline is gathering momentum. This is because the continuous rise in prices in recent days has prompted profit-takers to sell, easing the pressure on the market. At the same time, yarn sales have become sluggish. From the afternoon until closing, rumors circulated in the market, and as the news improved, the selling intensified, causing each month's contract to plunge by more than two yuan. In reality, the rise in recent days has been too drastic, and this kind of temporary reaction is to be expected.

Spot Yarn Bears Already Unloading Goods

In the morning session for spot yarn, as the delivery date for the current month approached, bears with 2,000 bales of Five Blessings Shepherd yarn from twenty entities and 100 bales of Red Dipper Star yarn from ten entities began unloading into warehouses. This eased the pressure somewhat. In addition, as news about the current situation improved, government bonds rose, and margin calls fell, there were fewer buyers in the market, and the market gradually declined. The results for spot yarn showed that each month's contract fell by 2.1 to 3 yuan compared to the previous day's closing price, but the current month only fell by 8 jiao. In the afternoon session, the bullish force for the current month remained strong, and the market outlook was still upward. However, distant futures were more stable, with little fluctuation in the second and third positions. By the time of closing, reports indicated that spot yarn transactions were not smooth. With improving news circulating in the market, sellers rushed in like a tide, causing prices to fall by more than 2 yuan, with distant months breaking through the 40 yuan mark. The results showed that each month's contract fell again by 2.7 to 1.9 yuan compared to the morning session's closing price, while the current month fell by 2 jiao. Piece Goods: Cotton Cloth Also Declining Rapidly; Traders Eagerly Sell Off Low-Priced Inventory While Prices are High 191

The trend in the cloth market is increasingly weak. As the situation in Shaanxi gradually eases, people's mood is relaxing. Yesterday, white fine cloth fell by 1 to 1.5 jiao per piece, and fine twill fell by 5 fen to 1 jiao per piece. Grains: Dalian Prices Report a Decline; Flour Suddenly Drops in the Afternoon 192

In yesterday's flour market, after the morning opening, the market for each month's contract showed an initial rise followed by a decline. As the price of foreign wheat was reported higher, Chicago rose by 2 to 3 jiao, and the distant month rose by a small 2 jiao. Canadian wheat rose by 3 to 7 jiao. Therefore, after opening, because foreign wheat rose sharply, general outsiders actively covered their positions, but the bulls ultimately felt that there were fewer and fewer actual chips, and there was no possibility of continuing to fix foreign wheat. Therefore, new records were seen repeatedly, and both insiders and outsiders believed that it was temporarily impossible. Each month continued to rise by 2 to 3 fen compared to the previous day. By the time the afternoon session opened, the market atmosphere suddenly became loose because the Shaanxi Incident might be resolved, and rumors spread that a certain country had a coup and Dalian prices were falling. Therefore, as these rumors suddenly arose, each month fell back one after another, falling back 5 to 6 fen compared to the morning's highest price and reaching about 1 to 3 fen compared to the previous day's closing price.

Continuous Selling Leads to an Intensified Decline in Soybean Cake 194

In the afternoon, there were widespread rumors that a certain country had unrest, and telegrams from Dalian repeatedly reported declines, causing chaos in the market. Both covering and new selling competed to sell off, and the market price fell sharply again. The final closing price for standard beans fell sharply by about 1 jiao to 2 jiao, standard oil fell by 8.5 jiao to 9.5 jiao, and standard cake also fell by a small 3 to 4 fen.

Good Price for Late Rice in Zhongguan, Worth More than a Jiao 195

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, shipments from various groups totaled over 90 numbers, with a total of 18,300 to 18,400 shi of goods. Among them, late rice accounted for over 40 numbers. Because of the scarcity of mid-grade goods, late rice was purchased very quietly, and high-quality materials were becoming lax. It is estimated that groups from Tianjin, Qingdao, Yantai, etc., purchased around 5,000 bags. The price of mid-grade goods rose by 1 jiao. Due to price increases, buyers and sellers could not agree on high-quality materials. It did not open until 6:00 PM, with a difference of about 5 fen up or down. Only 400 to 500 bags of thick japonica rice were purchased. However, sales on this street were still good, so the price also rose by a few fen to nearly 1 jiao. Du Yangjian also followed up by a few fen. Yinyuan wine shops saw movement and stood out again.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, over 50 ships arrived from various places downstream. The market for various goods was active in the morning but turned stagnant in the afternoon. High-quality white japonica rice was stable, and the price of mid-to-low-quality goods was slightly tight. Late rice purchases were still active, and the price increased by another 1 jiao on this street, with the price of 100 yuan also tightening by a few fen. Yangjian purchases were slightly stagnant, and the price fell by 3 to 4 fen. The price of the remaining goods was stable.

Merchants From Fujian and Guangdong Resume Purchasing Regular Rice 196

Yesterday, the local regular rice market saw increased activity, and people's minds were settled. Transactions also became more prosperous. As the situation has eased, merchants from Quanzhou have been actively purchasing early and late Jiangxi rice. Guangdong merchants continued to inquire about broken rice and rice flour. Henan merchants, who had been stagnant for many days, also resumed some business yesterday. Although the market was limited by ample inventory, prices were unable to rise. However, sales on this street were extremely prosperous throughout the day, with total transactions reaching nearly 10,000 bags. It is estimated that 5,000 bags of Jiangxi rice, over 3,000 bags of Hunan rice, and 1,855 bags of Ningbo, Shaoxing, and Wenzhou rice were sold.

Securities: Both Bulls and Short Covering Push Government Bonds Higher - Market Price Rises by Nearly Two Yuan 197

Yesterday's government bond market saw a turning point in the situation, and the bullish trend became more intense. The trend also showed a sudden prosperous appearance. As the Xi'an Incident is expected to ease, the market sentiment improved, and the market sentiment was extremely firm. Buying became more active, and major players covered their short positions and turned long. Amidst the enthusiastic market atmosphere, prices soared, and the rise was quite strong. Unified bonds have gradually returned to the prices during a period of calm. However, because the rise was too rapid, it is very easy to react. Yesterday morning, due to the improved situation and strong market sentiment, major players like 37th and 18th were buying aggressively, and the 10th was even more actively acquiring. Types E, D, and C all saw large amounts being absorbed, and the market price rose by 6 jiao to 1.25 yuan across the board. However, 22nd and 11th, etc., were selling off. The rise of types A and B was slightly slower, only rising by 3 to 5 jiao. The trend in the secondary market remained stable. 35th, 4th, and 50th, etc., sold off a lot, but retail investors and 18th and 45th, etc., continued to cover their short positions and buy in considerable amounts. Except for type E and C, which slightly fell by 5 fen, the rest rose by 5 fen to 2 jiao. Jin Chang even reached a high price of 60 yuan. In the afternoon session, short sellers were very eager to sell off, and 50th, 4th, and 35th, etc., all sold. However, 57th, 54th, and 6th, etc., continued to cover their short positions and buy in, so types E and C continued to rise by 1 jiao to 4 jiao. Types A and B for the next month, however, fell by 5 fen to 1.5 jiao. At closing, there was more good news about the situation, and market sentiment improved further. Major players such as 32nd and 43rd continued to buy in, and 18th alone absorbed a large amount. The market price improved again by 2 jiao to 7 jiao. The overall result was a uniform rise of 1 yuan to 1.9 yuan. The total number of transactions was 21,020,000 yuan. Finance: Margin Traders Show Little Interest; Many Bulls Liquidate; Spot Market Firm and Upward 198

Yesterday's gold market saw continued declines in pure gold, and the market was still stable. However, because buyers have been shaken and many bulls have been liquidating successively, it declined steadily. News also helped the bears. In the early morning, the overseas silver market saw rises in both England and the United States. Montry's forward silver price rose by 2.5 to 3.2 li. Exchange rates rose slightly. London raw silver fell by half a penny. The Central Bank's announced listing showed that both England and the United States were flat. The customs gold unit shrank by 2 li, and the standard margin price was listed at 1150.3 yuan. Pre-market trading opened outside the market, and Ding Kang sold slightly, retreating to around 61 yuan. Shengyuan Yongheng Yu Lai entered, rising to around 2 yuan. Fuxing Yong supplied at a high price, but the morning opening was still slightly higher. After the opening, people's minds suddenly became tired, and retail investors first sold off. Major short sellers took the opportunity to increase their positions and broke the 60 yuan mark. However, bulls also took action at low prices. The HSBC Bank's announced listing showed that both England and the United States were flat, and it once rebounded. Unfortunately, the bond market turned upward, and people's minds were downward, finally continuing to decline. The silver equalization tax was announced to rise by half a fen and then gradually stabilized. It also hovered at noon. In the afternoon market, a huge short covering caused a rebound, but due to the liquidation of many bulls, good news about the situation, and large short covering in the middle, it soon felt weak and finally plummeted. However, short sellers still covered after the low. The price of Indian silver initially rose by 1 anna, and the second time it fell back by a small 2 annas, finally hovering. The swap was posted by the bulls yesterday at 2.7 yuan, and the smelting cost continued to soar, having already been increased by 23 yuan yesterday. The day's market situation will be recorded below.

The morning opening was 1161.6 yuan, up 2 jiao from the previous closing. Retail investors and Fuxing Yongqing Fayongshengyuan sold off, retreating to 59.5 yuan. Tong Taichang Dadecheng Fuxing Yongyuan Mao Yongna listed the HSBC Bank's opening, with England and the United States both flat, rising to 60.6 yuan. A large number of Qiafeng Yong resold and retreated to 59 yuan. The silver balance tax was announced, rising by half a fen and then stabilizing. Tong Fengyong Ding Kang came to cover, rising to 9 yuan 6 jiao. Qingfa Yong limited the supply of positions, and the noon closing was 1159.5 yuan.

The afternoon market opened at 1159.7 yuan, and Fuxing Yongheng Yu Qiafeng Yong purchased positions, rising to 60.3 yuan. A large number of Qingfa Yong retail investors sold off, falling to 59 yuan. Fuxing Yong aggressively purchased, rising to 9.5 yuan. A large number of Fulings Yonghengchang Yonghengyu retail investors and Dadecheng sold off, retreating to 6.2 yuan. Yuan Mao Yong Qiafeng Yong went long at the low to 7.6 yuan. A large number of Ding Kang Dadecheng sold off, falling again to 6.3 yuan. Indian silver rolled small 1 anna, Qiafeng Yong purchased positions, rising to 7.5 yuan. Ding Kang continued to sell, and the closing was 1157 yuan. After the market closed, a large number, etc., slightly absorbed and stabilized.

The settlement price was listed by the Central Bank's standard gold price at 1150.3 yuan. According to the closing price, it was raised by about 10 yuan. The January record was 258 yuan, and the January price was 1160 yuan. The morning water replenishment was 1157 yuan, and the afternoon water replenishment was 1154 yuan. The spot market suddenly became firm again. The smelting cost was increased by 21 yuan to 23 yuan. Tongfen Heng successively sold to silver shops and other places for a total of about 600 taels, with a purchase price of 14 yuan. Tianjin goods were added 15 yuan, but there were no transactions. The swap was successively posted by Chunyuan Yongyuan Mao Yongshengyuan from 2.4 yuan to 2.7 yuan. Tongfen Heng Chengda made efforts to advance and then finalized.

Investigation Shanghai Price Index Rises (II) 199

(III) Import Price Index: The general index is 142.9, up 0.4% from last month and 0.1% from the same month last year. Comparing the three categories of indices with last month, raw materials and manufactured products have slightly increased, while consumer goods have slightly decreased. Raw materials have increased by 1.3%. Copper, lead, and tin have risen sharply overseas, and their prices in the city have followed suit, especially large lead bars, which have increased the most. The price per picul was $19.80 last month and has risen to $24.50 this month, an increase of 24%. Due to the impact of the American seamen's strike, the source of Douglas fir planks has been blocked, and they have risen along with Lauan planks. White coal and coal dross have also become firm and expensive due to the peak sales season. American wheat is too expensive to be sold in reality, and its virtual trading price is also higher than last month. The manufactured products index has increased by 1.7%, with most metal products rising. Foreign paper, sulfuric acid, and paraffin wax are becoming firm and expensive due to scarce inventory, wool yarn is becoming expensive due to costly raw materials, and glass is becoming firm and expensive due to low arrivals and high demand. Consumer goods have fallen by 0.4%. Flour has long been in a virtual trading state, and its price has risen along with domestic flour. Fresh oranges and macaroni are also rising due to the American seamen's strike, which has interrupted their supply, especially the price of fresh oranges has risen sharply. The selling price per box was $24 last month and has increased to $32 this month, an increase of one-third. Woolen goods are in short supply due to the peak sales season, and both arrivals and inventory are lacking, with firm asking prices. Linen and burlap sacks are also becoming expensive. However, the selling price of red and white sugar has slightly decreased, and feather silk and 1.6-foot velvet have also fallen across the board, resulting in little change in this category of index. (To be continued)

British American Tobacco Company Settles Sterling, Foreign Exchange Still Tight Due to Chinese Merchants Unloading 200

Yesterday, the foreign exchange market was somewhat tight due to Chinese merchants' reluctance to sell. Although British American Tobacco Company settled, it remained loose. Initially, according to overseas telegrams, both near and far dates for London large bars rose by 0.0625, and New York silver rose by 0.025. The forward silver price in Chow Deh Lee rose by 2.5 to 3 li. London raw gold fell by 1.5 pence. Sterling rose against the US dollar by 0.0125, remained unchanged against the French franc, the US dollar rose against sterling by 0.0625, and rose against the French franc by 0.06225. The Central Bank's official exchange rates were announced, with sterling and the US dollar remaining unchanged. The Customs Gold Unit fell by 0.03. The foreign exchange market opened in the morning with the near-term selling price of sterling at 1 shilling 2 pence 40625, and the US dollar at 29.5 yuan. Compared to the previous close, sterling loosened by 0.03125, and the US dollar remained unchanged. After the opening, the Japanese Bank of China bought sterling and sold Japanese yen. HSBC announced its official exchange rates, with both sterling and the US dollar remaining unchanged. Later, market sentiment weakened, and Chinese merchants started selling. Although the silver equalization tax rose by 0.005, the forward market loosened. Mercantile Bank sold sterling, and the market could not sustain itself at noon. Later, banks came back to settle. British American Tobacco Company also settled sterling. Although market sentiment was weak, the process was still stable. Indian silver initially rose by 1 anna, then retreated twice by 2 annas and fluctuated. The closing price for near-term sales was sterling at 1 shilling 2 pence 4375, and the US dollar at 29.5 yuan. Compared to the previous close, sterling loosened by 0.0625, the US dollar remained unchanged, and forward rates each tightened by 0.0625. Chinese merchants sold 60,000 sterling and 200,000 US dollars. The transaction records for today are as follows:

The morning opening price for near-term sterling was 1 shilling 2 pence 90625. Mitsui bought March futures at 0.025. Mercantile sold March futures to Yokohama Specie Bank at 0.025. Citibank China bought January futures at 0.0375. Mercantile bought March futures at 0.028125 and 0.03125. Mercantile sold January futures to Citibank Shanghai Zhejiang Yokohama Specie Bank at 0.0375. Shanghai bought December futures at 0.04375. Banque Belge pour l'Etranger bought January futures at 0.0375. Later, Mercantile bought March futures at 0.028125. Mercantile sold December futures to British American Tobacco Company at 0.040625 and February futures at 0.028125. Chase sold January futures at 0.0375. HSBC sold December futures at 0.040625. Banque Franco-Chinoise sold January futures to Mercantile at 0.034375. Netherlands Trading Society sold February futures at 0.028125. All of these were settled by British American Tobacco Company. The selling prices quoted by brokers were sterling at 1 shilling 2 pence 4375 for spot goods, 0.040625 for December futures, 0.0375 for January futures, 0.03125 for February futures, and 0.025 for March futures, with a slight increase in the buying price.

The morning opening price for the US dollar was 29.5 yuan. Shanghai sold February futures at 0.025, and bought January futures at 0.0375. Citibank sold February futures to Yokohama Specie Bank at 0.025. Shanghai bought February futures at 0.03125. Yokohama Specie Bank bought February futures at 0.03125. Citibank took March futures at 0.025. The noon closing price for near-term sales was 29.5 yuan. Later, Banque Franco-Chinoise bought February futures at 0.03125. Mercantile bought March futures at 0.01875. Chase sold January futures at 0.0375. Citibank bought spot goods at 0.05625. The closing selling prices were 29.5 yuan for spot goods, 0.04375 for December futures, 0.0375 for January futures, 0.025 for February futures, and 0.0125 for March futures, with an increase of 0.0625 for the buying price.

Silk and Tea Prices Fall Far Below Previous Levels 201

Yesterday, overseas silk markets in Japan and the United States declined again. New York standard silk for December fell by 0.03, and May futures fell by 0.02. Yokohama spot prices fell by 10 yuan, and April futures fell by 11 yuan. Lyon silk prices remained unchanged. New York prices rose slightly, but silk trading remained strained. Yesterday, the local silk market remained cautious. Sales of white filature silk were very limited, while grey silk sales were slightly better, but silk prices were far below previous levels (grey silk was previously sold at 415 yuan before October). In addition, sales of user silk were also low, and market sentiment turned sluggish again.

Metals: Huisheng Iron Fixed Price Rises to Nine Gold Yuan 202

The overseas fixed price of Huisheng Iron suddenly rose to nine gold yuan yesterday (per box of 200 pounds), more than seven gold jiao higher than before. Local industry peers, due to the high fixed price, found it difficult to sell, so they generally did not dare to purchase it, resulting in little business. It is said that after the overseas surge, the Shanghai market has also been driven up by 1-2 yuan. For example, steel plate factories were selling at 38.5 yuan, Xin Steel Factory at 37 yuan, and "Ye Ji Huo" at 16 yuan, but due to the rapid price increase, transactions were also very rare.

Sugar Market: New Chaoqing Production Prices Continue to Loosen 203

Yesterday, the sugar market trend was flat. The Guild's quoted price for spot No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar was 21.6 yuan, and the re-export price was 6.2 yuan. The spot price for Dongbai No. 4 was 21.6 yuan, No. 8 was 21.3 yuan, and No. 9 YRO mark was 21.1 yuan, with re-export prices of 6 yuan, 6.4 yuan for No. 4, and 6.2 yuan for No. 8. The spot price for local factory refined white sugar Dahua No. 1 was 20.4 yuan, and the prices for Nos. 2, 3, 4, and 5 remained the same. Only a few dozen bags of new Chaoqing sugar were offered by the Chao gang, priced at 13.5 yuan, which was 0.2 yuan lower than the price offered for road goods the previous day. It is also heard that Shantou production prices continue to fall, and the market is expected to decline further.

The joint venture company held its third tender for Guangdong sugar this week, with a total quota of less than 6,000 bags. 710 bags of Shunde factory Five Rams coarse white sugar were sold at 21.3 yuan, and 335 bags of Shantou sugar were sold at 20.9 yuan, with 120 bags sold at 20.7 yuan. The remaining new white sugar and medium granulated white sugar at the original price were not sold.

Miscellaneous News: Haikou Rubber Out of Stock 204

Due to a prolonged lack of deliveries, Haikou rubber prices have been rising, reaching over 10 yuan. At the current market price, each dan (unit of weight) can be sold for 65-66 yuan. According to information from the production area, due to the cold weather, production has temporarily ceased. All existing stock is being shipped to Guangzhou for sale, as prices there are higher than in Shanghai, resulting in no further deliveries to Shanghai and a consequent stockout.

The Permanence and Temporality of Youth 205

— Dan Xing

There is nothing more precious in life than youth. Everyone has youth, but only those who can make use of it, live up to it, and maintain it forever can be considered exceptional and lead a fulfilling life. A woman's youth is an especially important stage in her life, a time when her happiness or misfortune, her expansive or narrow future, is determined. To "maintain youth" does not mean that women should apply makeup and wear fashionable clothes for the rest of their lives. Such artificial and material attempts at preserving youth are futile. We would find it ridiculous and laughable to see an old woman with permed hair and lipstick!

Since there are no immortals in this world, there is no magic to stop aging and decay. The youth that is visible in age and appearance is temporary. Permanent youth resides in a cheerful spirit and a fulfilling life. When your inner self and your environment are in harmony, you feel the vitality and joy of youth, even if you are middle-aged or near death.

A young woman is like a budding flower, full of fiery vitality and flourishing growth. However, these fragile shoots must be carefully nurtured, as they cannot withstand even the slightest damage. They need to be nurtured in gentle sunlight and abundant rain. But many self-proclaimed intelligent women are too eager to flaunt their youth. They often immerse this great, pure, and precious time in scarlet dreams. What do they gain in the end? Only disappointment, sorrow, bitterness, resentment, negativity, regret... and the hollow longing for a dream. After experiencing disappointment in marriage and love, they blame society for all their sins and misfortunes, claiming that society has deceived them.

If every woman could use reason to overcome the impulses of emotion, calm and complex thoughts, a serious and dignified attitude, a broad and sharp vision, and a steady and deliberate pace to resolve her ideal career and marriage during her youth, she would be able to obtain permanent happiness like that of youth, even though her actual youth has been entirely offered and consumed in her marriage and career. Spiritual youth will never disappear. What, then, is the value of fleeting pleasure and happiness!

Please do not yearn for unripe fruit. When you taste its bitter and sour flavor, you will regret it. Youth is like an express train speeding along the tracks of life. If you are not careful, you will miss your stop. This is definitely not the time to dream scarlet dreams.

Amidst the Enthusiastic Support for Suiyuan, a Nameless Lady Worthy of Our Emulation 206

— Jun Peng

The resistance in Suiyuan has already begun. A certain faction is now coercing traitorous Chinese collaborators to attack Suiyuan, our country's foremost line of defense. Fortunately, our loyal General Fu Zuoyi is leading his brave soldiers in a bloody battle against the enemy. We who are in the rear cannot join the front lines to fight the enemy like the women of Abyssinia. Of course, everyone should do their part for the country and the nation, expressing some patriotic enthusiasm. Here, I report to 200 million female compatriots! Good news worth emulating:

According to a Xiamen dispatch in this newspaper on December 1st, on the morning of the 25th of last month, a woman stood in front of the Jiangsheng Newspaper office, reading the posted newspapers for about half an hour. She then entered the office and took off the gold ring she was wearing, asking the newspaper to sell it for her and send the proceeds to Suiyuan to comfort the anti-enemy soldiers on the front lines. However, the woman did not give her name; the receipt only stated "anonymous." The newspaper then took the ring to a jewelry store, where it was valued at seven yuan. The newspaper also announced the public sale of the ring. Subsequently, Wu Potang offered to purchase it for fourteen yuan. Fu Weige, the manager of the Xiamen He Auto Company, offered twenty yuan to purchase the ring as a gift for his wife. There were also five young siblings named Zhang, Zhang Guomei, Zhang Jiamei, Zhang Yiwei, Zhang Qiumei, and Zhang Hengwei, who were willing to use their accumulated candy money of twenty-eight yuan to purchase the anonymous lady's ring. The above-mentioned gentlemen and ladies are all patriotic comrades who enthusiastically support Suiyuan. Furthermore, the Zhang siblings stated that if someone was willing to offer a higher price, they were willing to relinquish it. Mr. Fu has already relinquished the ring to the Zhang siblings and did not take back the twenty yuan, hoping to raise more funds to provide more assistance to the soldiers on the front lines.

Dear female compatriots! What is your reaction after reading about the anonymous lady in Xiamen taking off her gold ring to support Suiyuan? Hey! Remember a few days ago, didn't the women of Italy use gold rings to save their country? Well, then, let's do it! Hurry up and donate your jewelry to the government to strengthen national defense. Furthermore, Ms. Hua Xu in this magazine previously requested that you all save on cosmetics, perms, decorations, entertainment, and other expenses to comfort the soldiers on the front lines. This is what we should promote as "using spare rings to save the country." Perhaps this anonymous lady is our initiator! I hope that 200 million female compatriots across the country will participate in the "gold ring to save the country" movement. I believe you will all be happy to emulate it!

The Life of Japanese Bus Conductresses 207

— Ji Yun

Japanese bus conductresses are the latest popular profession for Japanese women. Initially, after a commercial bus company in Tokyo hired women to sell tickets, business boomed. Consequently, Tokyo municipal buses and trams also used bus conductresses as a countermeasure. Now, bus conductresses are used for advertising all over Japan. Municipal bus conductresses are introduced by city council members and social workers, so strict selection is not possible. Commercial bus companies advertise for applicants and can select 20 out of over 500 people. Therefore, their appearance, figure, and health are better than those of municipal bus conductresses. About one-tenth (over 60 people) are graduates of higher girls' schools. The age of employment is from 16 to 18 years old, and they retire at 25, while municipal bus conductresses retire at 35.

The commercial bus company's bus conductresses receive 55 fen per day, a subsidy of 35 fen, and a commission of 26 per thousand for ticket sales. The municipal bus conductresses receive 8 jiao per day. Both earn about 30 yuan per month, with a maximum increase to 50 yuan. They work about 80 hours, with one day off every eight days. Young bus conductresses interact with male drivers and passengers all day long, which inevitably leads to youthful boredom and romantic incidents. Therefore, bus companies do not allow bus conductresses to live near the depot, and drivers and ticket sellers are rotated to prevent them from becoming too familiar. At the same time, supervisors disguise themselves as passengers to prevent incidents. After finishing work, bus conductresses must take a bath at the depot, not just to clean their bodies but also to check if they have hidden any money in their clothes. Each depot has two middle-aged women called "inspection site teachers." They not only have the power of life and death over the bus conductresses but also sometimes act as matchmakers. Because passengers who fall in love with bus conductresses often come to the depot to propose, the "inspection site teachers" become matchmakers.

The commercial bus company runs a Mingde Girls' School. All bus conductresses on vacation can attend free of charge, learning home economics, sewing, etiquette, national language, calligraphy, and other subjects. The municipal bus company also has floral arrangement instructors at each depot. In this way, the lives of Japanese bus conductresses are completely controlled by the company. In areas with more passengers, bus companies also send service girls to greet passengers. There are over 30 of them in Tokyo. They are the most beautiful and representative bus conductresses selected from the buses, and they serve at least as advertising. Standing gracefully on the streets of Tokyo, greeting passengers, is the latest tactic invented by the bus company.

The uniform of the municipal bus company's bus conductresses is a navy blue Western-style dress with a short top and a long skirt, which is very flattering. Each set costs 15 yuan. The municipal company quickly imitated them, but because they only cost five or six yuan ready-made, the bus conductresses were very dissatisfied. Japanese bus conductresses love to dress up. In addition to holding ticket clips, money bags, and scissors in their hands, they also have to take care of their hats and the corners of their clothes. Red lips, dark eyebrows, a few clear announcements of place names, and the swaying of their bodies in high-heeled shoes and the bus have captivated many passengers.

— (Huo Gu)

Women, you all occupy important positions in your families. Your every move directly affects your families and indirectly affects society and the country. But in the current situation, as long as we think of the brave soldiers fighting bloody battles in the icy and snowy wilderness, we in the rear should not still be using fireplaces for warmth.

You are all progressive women, and I believe you will all accept my small request.

Common Sense of Family Poison Prevention 210

— Lu Zhizun

How to Predict the Signs of a Poison Gas Attack and How to Avoid It:

(1) When people near the battlefield suddenly smell a strange odor, they should be wary of a poison gas attack.

(2) When people near the battlefield suddenly see a sky-covering fog, they should be wary of a poison gas attack.

(3) When people near the battlefield suddenly hear continuous loud noises, they should be wary of a poison gas attack.

(4) When flowers and plants in the home suddenly turn yellow and wither, they should be wary of a poison gas attack.

(5) When dogs, chickens, and small animals suddenly die on the streets, they should be wary of a poison gas attack.

(6) There is no need to worry during stormy weather. Quiet nights with no wind or when the wind is coming from the enemy's direction are ideal opportunities for the enemy to release poison gas.

(7) Poison gas is heavier than air and flows to low-lying areas. Therefore, it is unreasonable to hide in cellars or basements during a poison gas attack. You should quickly seek high ground to take shelter. Roofs, tall trees, tall towers, observation posts, and mountaintops are all safer.

(8) It is unreasonable to stand still when attacked by poison gas in the field. You must cover your mouth and nose with a wet cloth and run upwind, or you may be able to escape the range of the poison gas.

(9) It is unreasonable to open windows and doors to look around when attacked by poison gas indoors. You must quickly close the doors and windows tightly, and plug any leaks with wet paper or cloth. If there is already poison gas in the room, you can spray the prepared alkaline solution, such as sodium thiosulfate water, with a sprayer, or spray it in your mouth to eliminate the poison gas in the air.

(10) It is unreasonable to only close the doors and windows when the house is surrounded by poison gas. You must close each room door tightly. If someone goes in or out, use a poison gas protection spray to protect them each time a door is opened, and the door must be closed tightly immediately after going in or out.

Essential Knowledge for Housewives: Prevention and First Aid for Coal Poisoning 211

— Wang Shouqiu

The weather is getting cold! Most families are lighting their stoves. Wealthy families naturally use foreign stoves, but most families, due to economic constraints, can only burn coal balls for warmth. However, based on our past experience, the number of people who die from coal gas poisoning every year is considerable. Therefore, I am here to advise housewives to pay special attention to burning coal balls to avoid unfortunate events. Now, I will write about a few points that must be paid attention to when burning coal balls, and first aid methods for those who are unfortunately poisoned by coal gas. This can also be said to be essential knowledge for housewives.

It is best to light coal balls outside and move them into the room after the coal gas has dissipated. The windows in the room must be ventilated and must not be closed tightly. When sleeping, the stove must be moved outside. Otherwise, a basin of cold water should be placed in the room, because cold water can absorb coal gas. But I always think that moving it outside is the most appropriate.

If someone is poisoned by coal gas, immediately carry the person to a place where the air is flowing, and have him lie on his back while loosening his clothes. Give him sauerkraut brine to drink. The older the sauerkraut brine, the better. It is very effective to use it to treat someone poisoned by coal gas. At the same time, call a doctor for treatment. If the doctor is too far away, you can first apply artificial respiration to help him gradually restore his breathing, which can be saved, except for those who have been poisoned for too long. In short, in the event of such an unfortunate event, do not panic, but quickly try to find sauerkraut brine, perform artificial respiration, and quickly call a doctor. If you delay, it will be difficult to save!

Maids often like to secretly move the coal ball stove into the bedroom. Some even add a few more coal balls before going to bed because they are afraid of the cold. This is the most dangerous thing. Most people who are poisoned by coal gas are like this. Therefore, housewives must strictly warn their maids, explain in detail, and often check to avoid unfortunate events from happening.
